        #wps-generator ::-webkit-scrollbar-track { background: transparent; }
        #wps-generator ::-webkit-scrollbar-thumb { background: rgba(123, 140, 222, 0.2); border-radius: 3px; }
    </style>


    <!-- Employer Card -->
    <div class="wps-card">
        <h1 class="wps-title">🇦🇪 WPS SIF Generator</h1>
        <p class="wps-subtitle">UAE Wages Protection System — Compliant file generation</p>


        <div class="wps-grid-2 wps-mb-16">
            <div>
                <label>Employer ID (MoL)</label>
                <input type="text" id="wpsEmployerId" placeholder="Enter MoL ID">
            </div>
            <div>
                <label>Employer Bank</label>
                <select id="wpsEmployerBank">
                    <option value="">Select bank...</option>
                </select>

        </div>


        <div>
            <label>Salary Month</label>

        </div>

    <!-- Employees Card -->

            <button class="wps-btn wps-btn-primary" onclick="WPS.addEmployee()">+ Add Employee</button>

        <div id="wpsEmployeesContainer"></div>
    </div>


    <!-- Download & Summary Card -->

            <div class="wps-download-group">

                <div class="wps-dropdown" id="wpsDownloadMenu">

                <span class="wps-summary-sep">&nbsp;|&nbsp;</span>

                <button class="wps-btn wps-btn-secondary" onclick="WPS.closePreview()">✕ Close</button>

                <button class="wps-btn wps-btn-primary" onclick="WPS.downloadSIF()">⬇️ Download SIF</button>

<script>
(function() {
    var banks = [
        { n: "Abu Dhabi Commercial Bank (ADCB)", c: "600310101" },
        { n: "Abu Dhabi Islamic Bank (ADIB)", c: "405010101" },
        { n: "Ajman Bank", c: "805740101" },
        { n: "Commercial Bank of Dubai (CBD)", c: "102320150" },
        { n: "Dubai Islamic Bank (DIB)", c: "802420101" },
        { n: "Emirates Islamic Bank", c: "703420114" },
        { n: "Emirates NBD Bank", c: "202620103" },
        { n: "First Abu Dhabi Bank (FAB)", c: "803510106" },
        { n: "HSBC Bank Middle East", c: "302020120" },
        { n: "Mashreqbank", c: "203320101" },
        { n: "National Bank of Fujairah", c: "703820101" },
        { n: "RAKBANK", c: "104060106" },
        { n: "Sharjah Islamic Bank", c: "404130101" },
        { n: "Standard Chartered Bank", c: "504420120" },
        { n: "WIO Bank", c: "808610001" },
        { n: "Al Ansari Exchange", c: "720610101", t: 1 },
        { n: "UAE Exchange", c: "929110101", t: 1 },
    ].sort(function(a, b) { return a.n.localeCompare(b.n); });


    var employees = [createEmployee()];
    var nextId = Date.now() + 1;


    function createEmployee() {
        return {
            id: Date.now(),
            visaId: "",
            visaIdManual: false,
            empBank: "",
            iban: "",
            startDate: "",
            endDate: "",
            basic: "",
            housing: "",
            transport: "",
            other: "",
            deductions: "",
            leaveDays: "0",
        };
    }


    function addEmployee() {
        var last = employees[employees.length - 1];
        var newEmp = createEmployee();
        newEmp.id = nextId++;
        if (last) {
            newEmp.startDate = last.startDate;
            newEmp.endDate = last.endDate;
        }
        employees.push(newEmp);
        renderEmployees();
    }


    function removeEmployee(id) {
        if (employees.length > 1) {
            employees = employees.filter(function(e) { return e.id !== id; });
            renderEmployees();
        }
    }


    function updateEmployee(id, field, value) {
        employees = employees.map(function(e) {
            if (e.id === id) {
                var updated = Object.assign({}, e);
                updated[field] = value;
                if (field === "iban" && !e.visaIdManual) {
                    var clean = value.replace(/\s/g, "").toUpperCase();
                    if (clean.length >= 21) {
                        updated.visaId = clean.substring(10, 21);
                    }
                    var prefix = clean.substring(4, 7);
                    var bankMap = {
                        "033": "203320101",
                        "030": "600310101",
                        "035": "803510106",
                        "024": "802420101",
                        "026": "202620103",
                        "027": "803510106",
                        "038": "703820101",
                        "040": "104060106",
                        "050": "405010101",
                        "086": "808610001",
                    };
                    if (bankMap[prefix] && !e.empBank) {
                        updated.empBank = bankMap[prefix];
                    }
                }
                if (field === "visaId") {
                    updated.visaIdManual = true;
                }
                return updated;
            }
            return e;
        });


        if (field === "iban") {
            renderEmployees();
        } else {
            updateSummary();
        }
    }


    function calcDays(start, end) {
        if (!start || !end) return 0;
        var s = new Date(start), e = new Date(end);
        return Math.max(0, Math.ceil((e - s) / 86400000) + 1);
    }


    function calcTotal(emp) {
        var basic = parseFloat(emp.basic) || 0;
        var housing = parseFloat(emp.housing) || 0;
        var transport = parseFloat(emp.transport) || 0;
        var other = parseFloat(emp.other) || 0;
        var deductions = parseFloat(emp.deductions) || 0;
        return basic + housing + transport + other - deductions;
    }


    function escapeAttr(str) {
        return (str || '').replace(/"/g, '&quot;').replace(/</g, '&lt;').replace(/>/g, '&gt;');
    }


    function renderEmployees() {
        var container = document.getElementById('wpsEmployeesContainer');
        container.innerHTML = '';


        employees.forEach(function(emp, idx) {
            var card = document.createElement('div');
            card.className = 'wps-emp-card';
            card.innerHTML =
                '<div class="wps-emp-header">' +
                    '<span class="wps-emp-title">Employee #' + (idx + 1) + '</span>' +
                    '<div class="wps-emp-header-right">' +
                        '<span class="wps-total-badge" id="wpsBadge-' + emp.id + '">Net: AED ' + calcTotal(emp).toFixed(2) + '</span>' +
                        (employees.length > 1 ? '<button class="wps-btn-remove" onclick="WPS.removeEmployee(' + emp.id + ')">✕ Remove</button>' : '') +
                    '</div>' +
                '</div>' +


                '<div class="wps-grid-2 wps-mb-12">' +
                    '<div>' +
                        '<label>IBAN</label>' +
                        '<input type="text" value="' + escapeAttr(emp.iban) + '" placeholder="AE..." oninput="WPS.updateEmployee(' + emp.id + ', \'iban\', this.value)">' +
                    '</div>' +
                    '<div>' +
                        '<label>Employee Bank</label>' +
                        '<select onchange="WPS.updateEmployee(' + emp.id + ', \'empBank\', this.value)" id="wpsEmpBank-' + emp.id + '">' +
                            '<option value="">Select...</option>' +
                        '</select>' +
                    '</div>' +
                '</div>' +


                '<div class="wps-grid-3 wps-mb-12">' +
                    '<div>' +
                        '<label>Visa/Labour ID</label>' +
                        '<input type="text" value="' + escapeAttr(emp.visaId) + '" placeholder="Auto from IBAN" oninput="WPS.updateEmployee(' + emp.id + ', \'visaId\', this.value)">' +
                    '</div>' +
                    '<div>' +
                        '<label>Start Date</label>' +
                        '<input type="date" value="' + emp.startDate + '" onchange="WPS.updateEmployee(' + emp.id + ', \'startDate\', this.value)">' +
                    '</div>' +
                    '<div>' +
                        '<label>End Date</label>' +
                        '<input type="date" value="' + emp.endDate + '" onchange="WPS.updateEmployee(' + emp.id + ', \'endDate\', this.value)">' +
                    '</div>' +
                '</div>' +


                '<div class="wps-grid-3">' +
                    '<div>' +
                        '<label>Basic Salary</label>' +
                        '<input type="number" value="' + emp.basic + '" placeholder="0.00" oninput="WPS.updateEmployee(' + emp.id + ', \'basic\', this.value)">' +
                    '</div>' +
                    '<div>' +
                        '<label>Housing</label>' +
                        '<input type="number" value="' + emp.housing + '" placeholder="0.00" oninput="WPS.updateEmployee(' + emp.id + ', \'housing\', this.value)">' +
                    '</div>' +
                    '<div>' +
                        '<label>Transport</label>' +
                        '<input type="number" value="' + emp.transport + '" placeholder="0.00" oninput="WPS.updateEmployee(' + emp.id + ', \'transport\', this.value)">' +
                    '</div>' +
                    '<div>' +
                        '<label>Other Allow.</label>' +
                        '<input type="number" value="' + emp.other + '" placeholder="0.00" oninput="WPS.updateEmployee(' + emp.id + ', \'other\', this.value)">' +
                    '</div>' +
                    '<div>' +
                        '<label>Deductions</label>' +
                        '<input type="number" value="' + emp.deductions + '" placeholder="0.00" oninput="WPS.updateEmployee(' + emp.id + ', \'deductions\', this.value)">' +
                    '</div>' +
                    '<div>' +
                        '<label>Leave Days</label>' +
                        '<input type="number" value="' + emp.leaveDays + '" placeholder="0" oninput="WPS.updateEmployee(' + emp.id + ', \'leaveDays\', this.value)">' +
                    '</div>' +
                '</div>';
            container.appendChild(card);


            var bankSel = card.querySelector('#wpsEmpBank-' + emp.id);
            banks.forEach(function(b) {
                var opt = document.createElement('option');
                opt.value = b.c;
                opt.textContent = b.n;
                if (b.c === emp.empBank) opt.selected = true;
                bankSel.appendChild(opt);
            });
        });


        updateSummary();
    }


    function updateSummary() {
        var total = employees.reduce(function(sum, e) { return sum + calcTotal(e); }, 0);
        var salaryMonth = document.getElementById('wpsSalaryMonth').value;


        document.getElementById('wpsEmpCount').textContent = employees.length;
        document.getElementById('wpsTotalEmpCount').textContent = employees.length;
        document.getElementById('wpsTotalPayroll').textContent = total.toFixed(2);
        document.getElementById('wpsPeriodDisplay').textContent = salaryMonth || 'Not set';


        employees.forEach(function(emp) {
            var badge = document.getElementById('wpsBadge-' + emp.id);
            if (badge) badge.textContent = 'Net: AED ' + calcTotal(emp).toFixed(2);
        });
    }


    function generateSIF() {
        var employerId = document.getElementById('wpsEmployerId').value;
        var employerBank = document.getElementById('wpsEmployerBank').value;
        var salaryMonth = document.getElementById('wpsSalaryMonth').value;


        var content = "";
        var fileDate = new Date().toISOString().split("T")[0];
        var fileTime = new Date().toTimeString().substring(0, 5).replace(":", "");
        var monthParts = salaryMonth.split("-");
        var salMonth = monthParts[1] + "-" + monthParts[0];


        employees.forEach(function(emp) {
            var days = calcDays(emp.startDate, emp.endDate);
            var variable =
                (parseFloat(emp.housing) || 0) +
                (parseFloat(emp.transport) || 0) +
                (parseFloat(emp.other) || 0);
            content += "EDR," + emp.visaId.padStart(14, "0") + "," + emp.empBank + "," + emp.iban.replace(/\s/g, "").toUpperCase() + "," + emp.startDate + "," + emp.endDate + "," + days + "," + parseFloat(emp.basic || 0).toFixed(2) + "," + variable.toFixed(2) + "," + parseFloat(emp.deductions || 0).toFixed(2) + "\n";
        });


        var totalSalary = employees.reduce(function(sum, e) { return sum + calcTotal(e); }, 0);
        content += "SCR," + employerId.padStart(13, "0") + "," + employerBank + "," + fileDate + "," + fileTime + "," + salMonth + "," + employees.length + "," + totalSalary.toFixed(2);


        return content;
    }


    function downloadFile(content, filename, type) {
        type = type || "text/plain";
        var blob = new Blob(["\uFEFF" + content], { type: type + ";charset=utf-8" });
        var url = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
        var a = document.createElement("a");
        a.href = url;
        a.download = filename;
        a.click();
        URL.revokeObjectURL(url);
    }


    function downloadSIF() {
        var salaryMonth = document.getElementById('wpsSalaryMonth').value;
        var content = generateSIF();
        var filename = "WPS_" + salaryMonth + "_" + Date.now() + ".SIF";
        downloadFile(content, filename);
    }


    function generateCSV(format) {
        var employerId = document.getElementById('wpsEmployerId').value;
        var employerBank = document.getElementById('wpsEmployerBank').value;
        var salaryMonth = document.getElementById('wpsSalaryMonth').value;
        var fileDate = new Date().toISOString().split("T")[0];
        var monthParts = salaryMonth.split("-");
        var csv = "";


        if (format === "wio") {
            csv = "Employee_ID,Bank_Code,IBAN,Start_Date,End_Date,Days_Worked,Leave_Days,Basic_Salary,Variable_Pay,Deductions,Net_Salary\n";
            employees.forEach(function(emp) {
                var days = calcDays(emp.startDate, emp.endDate);
                var variable = (parseFloat(emp.housing) || 0) + (parseFloat(emp.transport) || 0) + (parseFloat(emp.other) || 0);
                var net = calcTotal(emp);
                csv += emp.visaId.padStart(14, "0") + "," + emp.empBank + "," + emp.iban.replace(/\s/g, "").toUpperCase() + "," + emp.startDate.replace(/-/g, "") + "," + emp.endDate.replace(/-/g, "") + "," + days + "," + (emp.leaveDays || 0) + "," + parseFloat(emp.basic || 0).toFixed(2) + "," + variable.toFixed(2) + "," + parseFloat(emp.deductions || 0).toFixed(2) + "," + net.toFixed(2) + "\n";
            });
        } else if (format === "enbd") {
            csv = "Record_Type,Employee_ID,Agent_Code,IBAN,Pay_Start,Pay_End,Days,Fixed_Amount,Variable_Amount,Deductions\n";
            employees.forEach(function(emp) {
                var days = calcDays(emp.startDate, emp.endDate);
                var variable = (parseFloat(emp.housing) || 0) + (parseFloat(emp.transport) || 0) + (parseFloat(emp.other) || 0);
                csv += "EDR," + emp.visaId.padStart(14, "0") + "," + emp.empBank + "," + emp.iban.replace(/\s/g, "").toUpperCase() + "," + emp.startDate + "," + emp.endDate + "," + days + "," + parseFloat(emp.basic || 0).toFixed(2) + "," + variable.toFixed(2) + "," + parseFloat(emp.deductions || 0).toFixed(2) + "\n";
            });
            var totalSalary = employees.reduce(function(sum, e) { return sum + calcTotal(e); }, 0);
            csv += "SCR," + employerId.padStart(13, "0") + "," + employerBank + "," + fileDate + ",," + monthParts[1] + "-" + monthParts[0] + "," + employees.length + "," + totalSalary.toFixed(2) + ",";
        } else if (format === "fab") {
            csv = "Employee_ID,Bank_Routing_Code,IBAN,Period_Start,Period_End,Working_Days,Basic_Salary,Allowances,Deductions,Total_Salary\n";
            employees.forEach(function(emp) {
                var days = calcDays(emp.startDate, emp.endDate);
                var allowances = (parseFloat(emp.housing) || 0) + (parseFloat(emp.transport) || 0) + (parseFloat(emp.other) || 0);
                var total = calcTotal(emp);
                csv += emp.visaId.padStart(14, "0") + "," + emp.empBank + "," + emp.iban.replace(/\s/g, "").toUpperCase() + "," + emp.startDate + "," + emp.endDate + "," + days + "," + parseFloat(emp.basic || 0).toFixed(2) + "," + allowances.toFixed(2) + "," + parseFloat(emp.deductions || 0).toFixed(2) + "," + total.toFixed(2) + "\n";
            });
        } else {
            csv = "Employee_ID,Bank_Code,IBAN,Start_Date,End_Date,Days,Basic_Salary,Variable_Pay,Deductions,Net_Salary\n";
            employees.forEach(function(emp) {
                var days = calcDays(emp.startDate, emp.endDate);
                var variable = (parseFloat(emp.housing) || 0) + (parseFloat(emp.transport) || 0) + (parseFloat(emp.other) || 0);
                var net = calcTotal(emp);
                csv += emp.visaId.padStart(14, "0") + "," + emp.empBank + "," + emp.iban.replace(/\s/g, "").toUpperCase() + "," + emp.startDate + "," + emp.endDate + "," + days + "," + parseFloat(emp.basic || 0).toFixed(2) + "," + variable.toFixed(2) + "," + parseFloat(emp.deductions || 0).toFixed(2) + "," + net.toFixed(2) + "\n";
            });
        }


        var formatNames = { wio: "WIO", enbd: "ENBD", fab: "FAB", standard: "CSV" };
        var salMo = document.getElementById('wpsSalaryMonth').value;
        var filename = "WPS_" + formatNames[format] + "_" + salMo + "_" + Date.now() + ".csv";
        downloadFile(csv, filename, "text/csv");
    }


    function toggleMenu() {
        var menu = document.getElementById('wpsDownloadMenu');
        var backdrop = document.getElementById('wpsSheetBackdrop');
        var isActive = menu.classList.contains('active');
        if (isActive) {
            menu.classList.remove('active');
            backdrop.classList.remove('active');
        } else {
            menu.classList.add('active');
            backdrop.classList.add('active');
        }
    }


    function closeMenu() {
        document.getElementById('wpsDownloadMenu').classList.remove('active');
        document.getElementById('wpsSheetBackdrop').classList.remove('active');
    }


    document.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
        var group = document.querySelector('#wps-generator .wps-download-group');
        if (group && !group.contains(e.target)) {
            closeMenu();
        }
    });


    function showPreview() {
        document.getElementById('wpsPreviewCode').textContent = generateSIF();
        document.getElementById('wpsPreviewModal').classList.add('active');
    }


    function closePreview() {
        document.getElementById('wpsPreviewModal').classList.remove('active');
    }


    document.getElementById('wpsPreviewModal').addEventListener('click', function(e) {
        if (e.target === this) closePreview();
    });


    document.addEventListener('keydown', function(e) {
        if (e.key === 'Escape') {
            closePreview();
            closeMenu();
        }
    });


    var sel = document.getElementById('wpsEmployerBank');
    banks.filter(function(b) { return !b.t; }).forEach(function(b) {
        var opt = document.createElement('option');
        opt.value = b.c;
        opt.textContent = b.n;
        sel.appendChild(opt);
    });


    document.getElementById('wpsSalaryMonth').addEventListener('change', updateSummary);


    renderEmployees();


    window.WPS = {
        addEmployee: addEmployee,
        removeEmployee: removeEmployee,
        updateEmployee: updateEmployee,
        downloadSIF: downloadSIF,
        generateCSV: generateCSV,
        showPreview: showPreview,
        closePreview: closePreview,
        toggleMenu: toggleMenu,
        closeMenu: closeMenu,
    };
})();
</script>

<style>

  <section class="dft-seo">
    <div class="dft-lang-fr">
      <h2>La <span>Corporate Tax UAE</span> en 2026</h2>
      <p>La Corporate Tax UAE est entrée en vigueur le 1er juin 2023 (Federal Decree-Law No. 47 of 2022). Taux standard : 0% jusqu'à AED 375 000 de bénéfice imposable, 9% au-delà. Trois régimes spéciaux existent : Small Business Relief, QFZP (Free Zones), et participation exemption pour holdings.</p>
      <h3>Small Business Relief (SBR)</h3>
      <p>Les entreprises avec un chiffre d'affaires &le; AED 3 000 000 peuvent opter pour le SBR : taux effectif 0%, mais obligation de produire une déclaration simplifiée. Valable jusqu'à fin 2026.</p>
      <h3>QFZP - Qualifying Free Zone Person</h3>
      <p>Conditions cumulatives : activité qualifiante, substance adéquate aux UAE, transfer pricing documenté, seuil de minimis (revenu non-qualifiant &le; 5% du total ou AED 5M), non-opt pour le 9%. Si toutes les conditions sont remplies : 0% sur le qualifying income, 9% sur le non-qualifying uniquement.</p>
      <h3>FAQ</h3>
      <div class="dft-faq-item"><div class="dft-faq-q">Quand dois-je déposer ma première déclaration CT ?<span>+</span></div><div class="dft-faq-a">Dans les 9 mois suivant la fin de la première période fiscale de la société. Exemple : exercice 01/01/2024-31/12/2024 → déclaration avant le 30/09/2025.</div></div>
      <div class="dft-faq-item"><div class="dft-faq-q">Puis-je reporter mes déficits ?<span>+</span></div><div class="dft-faq-a">Oui, sans limitation de durée, mais l'utilisation est plafonnée à 75% du bénéfice imposable de l'année où vous les imputez.</div></div>
    </div>
    <div class="dft-lang-en">
      <h2><span>UAE Corporate Tax</span> in 2026</h2>
      <p>UAE Corporate Tax came into force on 1 June 2023 (Federal Decree-Law No. 47 of 2022). Standard rate: 0% up to AED 375,000 taxable profit, 9% above. Three special regimes exist: Small Business Relief, QFZP (Free Zones), and participation exemption for holdings.</p>
      <h3>Small Business Relief (SBR)</h3>
      <p>Companies with revenue &le; AED 3,000,000 may elect SBR: effective rate 0%, with obligation to file a simplified return. Valid until end of 2026.</p>
      <h3>QFZP - Qualifying Free Zone Person</h3>
      <p>Cumulative conditions: qualifying activity, adequate substance in UAE, transfer pricing documentation, de minimis threshold (non-qualifying income &le; 5% of total or AED 5M), no opt for 9%. If all met: 0% on qualifying income, 9% on non-qualifying only.</p>
      <h3>FAQ</h3>
      <div class="dft-faq-item"><div class="dft-faq-q">When must I file my first CT return?<span>+</span></div><div class="dft-faq-a">Within 9 months after the end of the first tax period. Example: FY 01/01/2024-31/12/2024 → filing by 30/09/2025.</div></div>
      <div class="dft-faq-item"><div class="dft-faq-q">Can I carry forward losses?<span>+</span></div><div class="dft-faq-a">Yes, indefinitely, but usage is capped at 75% of the taxable profit of the year of offset.</div></div>
    </div>
  </section>

<script>
(function(){
  var root = document.getElementById('dftCtCalc');
  if(!root) return;
  var currentLang = 'fr';
  try {
    var saved = localStorage.getItem('daftime_lang');
    if(saved) currentLang = saved;
    else if(navigator.language && navigator.language.indexOf('en')===0) currentLang = 'en';
  } catch(e){}


  function setLang(l){
    currentLang = l;
    root.setAttribute('data-lang', l);
    try { localStorage.setItem('daftime_lang', l); } catch(e){}
    root.querySelectorAll('[data-fr]').forEach(function(el){
      var v = el.getAttribute('data-'+l);
      if(v !== null) el.innerHTML = v;
    });
    root.querySelectorAll('.dft-lang-btn').forEach(function(b){
      b.classList.toggle('active', b.getAttribute('data-lang') === l);
    });
    compute();
  }


  function n(id){ return parseFloat(document.getElementById(id).value) || 0; }
  function fmt(v){ return Math.round(v).toLocaleString(currentLang === 'en' ? 'en-US' : 'fr-FR'); }


  function compute(){
    var rev = n('dftRevenue'), profit = n('dftProfit');
    var regime = document.getElementById('dftRegime').value;
    var qi = n('dftQfzpInc'), qni = n('dftQfzpNonInc'), losses = n('dftLosses');
    var l = currentLang;
    var ct = 0, rate = '', alertMsg = '', rows = [];


    if(regime === 'sbr'){
      if(rev <= 3000000){
        ct = 0; rate = 'SBR · 0%';
        alertMsg = l === 'fr' ? '✓ Éligible SBR (CA ≤ AED 3M)' : '✓ SBR eligible (revenue ≤ AED 3M)';
      } else {
        var lossUse = Math.min(losses, profit * 0.75);
        var taxable = Math.max(profit - lossUse - 375000, 0);
        ct = taxable * 0.09;
        rate = '9%';
        alertMsg = l === 'fr' ? '⚠ CA dépasse AED 3M : SBR non applicable, taux 9% appliqué' : '⚠ Revenue exceeds AED 3M: SBR not applicable, 9% applied';
      }
    } else if(regime === 'qfzp'){
      var deMinPct = qi > 0 ? qni / (qi + qni) * 100 : 0;
      if(deMinPct > 5 && qni > 5000000){
        ct = profit * 0.09;
        alertMsg = l === 'fr' ? '⚠ Seuil de minimis dépassé : QFZP perdu, 9% sur tout le bénéfice' : '⚠ De minimis exceeded: QFZP lost, 9% on full profit';
        rate = '9%';
      } else {
        var taxableNon = Math.max(qni - 375000, 0);
        ct = taxableNon * 0.09;
        alertMsg = l === 'fr' ? '✓ QFZP préservé · 0% sur qualifying, 9% sur non-qualifying au-delà de 375K' : '✓ QFZP preserved · 0% on qualifying, 9% on non-qualifying above 375K';
        rate = '0% / 9%';
      }
    } else {
      var lossUse2 = Math.min(losses, profit * 0.75);
      var taxable2 = Math.max(profit - lossUse2 - 375000, 0);
      ct = taxable2 * 0.09;
      rate = taxable2 > 0 ? '9%' : '0% (< 375K)';
      rows.push({k: l === 'fr' ? 'Abattement SBR/Seuil' : 'SBR/Threshold relief', v: -375000});
      if(lossUse2 > 0) rows.push({k: l === 'fr' ? 'Déficit imputé' : 'Loss offset', v: -lossUse2});
      alertMsg = l === 'fr' ? 'ⓘ Régime mainland standard · seuil 375K + 9% au-delà' : 'ⓘ Mainland standard regime · 375K threshold + 9% above';
    }


    document.getElementById('dftResMain').textContent = 'AED ' + fmt(ct);
    document.getElementById('dftResSub').textContent = (l === 'fr' ? 'Taux effectif : ' : 'Effective rate: ') + rate;


    var html = '<div class="dft-result-row"><span>' + (l === 'fr' ? 'Bénéfice imposable' : 'Taxable profit') + '</span><span class="dft-val">' + fmt(profit) + '</span></div>';
    rows.forEach(function(r){
      html += '<div class="dft-result-row"><span>' + r.k + '</span><span class="dft-val">' + fmt(r.v) + '</span></div>';
    });
    html += '<div class="dft-result-row dft-highlight"><span>CORPORATE TAX</span><span class="dft-val">AED ' + fmt(ct) + '</span></div>';
    html += '<div class="dft-alert" style="margin-top:12px"><span class="dft-alert-icon">ⓘ</span><div>' + alertMsg + '</div></div>';
    document.getElementById('dftBreakdown').innerHTML = html;
  }


  root.querySelectorAll('.dft-lang-btn').forEach(function(b){
    b.addEventListener('click', function(){ setLang(b.getAttribute('data-lang')); });
  });


  root.querySelectorAll('.dft-faq-item').forEach(function(item){
    item.addEventListener('click', function(){ item.classList.toggle('open'); });
  });


  ['dftRevenue','dftProfit','dftRegime','dftQfzpInc','dftQfzpNonInc','dftLosses'].forEach(function(id){
    var el = document.getElementById(id);
    el.addEventListener('input', compute);
    el.addEventListener('change', compute);
  });


  setLang(currentLang);
})();
</script>

  <section class="dft-seo">
    <div class="dft-lang-fr">
      <h2>Le régime <span>QFZP</span> aux Émirats Arabes Unis</h2>
      <p>Le QFZP (Qualifying Free Zone Person) permet aux sociétés Free Zone de bénéficier d'un taux Corporate Tax de 0% sur le revenu qualifiant. Encadré par le Ministerial Decision No. 265 of 2023 et No. 139 of 2023.</p>
      <h3>Les 6 critères cumulatifs</h3>
      <ol><li>Être une personne morale constituée en Free Zone UAE</li><li>Avoir une substance adéquate (employés qualifiés, actifs, dépenses opérationnelles)</li><li>Percevoir un revenu qualifiant (activités listées)</li><li>Ne pas avoir opté pour le taux 9%</li><li>Respecter les règles de transfer pricing (Arms Length Principle + documentation)</li><li>Respecter le seuil de minimis (revenu non-qualifiant &le; 5% du total ou AED 5M)</li></ol>
      <h3>Activités qualifiantes</h3>
      <p>Fabrication, holding, shipping, trading de matières premières, services à des clients hors UAE, services à d'autres Free Zone Persons, treasury et financing pour le groupe, gestion de fonds, aviation, logistique.</p>
      <h3>Activités exclues</h3>
      <p>Transactions avec personnes physiques (sauf exceptions), banking et assurance (hors Free Zones régulées), activités immobilières (sauf immobilier commercial en Free Zone loué à une Free Zone Person).</p>
    </div>
    <div class="dft-lang-en">
      <h2>The <span>QFZP</span> regime in the UAE</h2>
      <p>QFZP (Qualifying Free Zone Person) enables Free Zone entities to enjoy a 0% Corporate Tax rate on qualifying income. Governed by Ministerial Decisions No. 265 of 2023 and No. 139 of 2023.</p>
      <h3>The 6 cumulative criteria</h3>
      <ol><li>Be a legal person incorporated in a UAE Free Zone</li><li>Maintain adequate substance (qualified staff, assets, operating expenditure)</li><li>Derive qualifying income (listed activities)</li><li>Not have elected to be subject to 9% CT</li><li>Comply with transfer pricing rules (Arm's Length Principle + documentation)</li><li>Meet the de minimis threshold (non-qualifying income &le; 5% of total or AED 5M)</li></ol>
      <h3>Qualifying activities</h3>
      <p>Manufacturing, holding, shipping, trading of qualifying commodities, services to non-UAE customers, services to other Free Zone Persons, treasury and financing for the group, fund management, aviation, logistics.</p>
      <h3>Excluded activities</h3>
      <p>Transactions with natural persons (except exceptions), banking and insurance (outside regulated Free Zones), real estate (except commercial real estate in Free Zone leased to a Free Zone Person).</p>
    </div>
  </section>

  function escapeHtml(s){

    root.setAttribute('data-lang', l);
    try { localStorage.setItem('daftime_lang', l); } catch(e){}
    root.querySelectorAll('[data-fr]').forEach(function(el){
      var v = el.getAttribute('data-'+l);
      if(v !== null) el.innerHTML = v;
    });
    root.querySelectorAll('.dft-lang-btn').forEach(function(b){
      b.classList.toggle('active', b.getAttribute('data-lang') === l);
    });
    if($('dftResultContainer').style.display === 'block'){
      showResult();
    } else {
      renderQ();
    }
  }


  function renderQ(){
    var qs = questions[currentLang] || questions.fr;
    var q = qs[cur];
    $('dftProgress').style.width = (cur / qs.length * 100) + '%';
    $('dftQCount').textContent = (currentLang === 'fr' ? 'Question ' : 'Question ') + (cur + 1) + ' / ' + qs.length;
    $('dftQText').textContent = q.q;
    $('dftQHint').textContent = q.h;
    var html = q.opts.map(function(o, i){
      var sel = answers[cur] === i ? ' selected' : '';
      return '<button type="button" class="dft-option' + sel + '" data-opt="' + i + '">' + escapeHtml(o) + '</button>';
    }).join('');
    $('dftOptions').innerHTML = html;
    $('dftOptions').querySelectorAll('[data-opt]').forEach(function(btn){
      btn.addEventListener('click', function(){
        var i = parseInt(btn.getAttribute('data-opt'), 10);
        select(i);
      });
    });
    $('dftPrevBtn').disabled = cur === 0;
  }


  function select(i){
    var qs = questions[currentLang] || questions.fr;
    answers[cur] = i;
    renderQ();
    setTimeout(function(){
      if(cur < qs.length - 1){
        cur++;
        renderQ();
      } else {
        showResult();
      }
    }, 300);
  }


  function prev(){
    if(cur > 0){
      cur--;
      renderQ();
    }
  }


  function showResult(){
    var qs = questions[currentLang] || questions.fr;
    var total = 0, max = 0, elim = false;
    qs.forEach(function(q, i){
      var a = answers[i];
      if(a === undefined) return;
      total += q.w[a];
      max += Math.max.apply(null, q.w);
      if(q.elim[a]) elim = true;
    });
    var pct = max > 0 ? (total / max * 100) : 0;
    $('dftQuizContainer').style.display = 'none';
    $('dftResultContainer').style.display = 'block';
    var head = $('dftResHead');
    var status, sub;
    if(elim || pct < 50){
      head.className = 'dft-result-header danger';
      status = currentLang === 'fr' ? 'Non éligible' : 'Not eligible';
      sub = currentLang === 'fr' ? 'Critères rédhibitoires non remplis' : 'Deal-breaker criteria not met';
    } else if(pct >= 85){
      head.className = 'dft-result-header success';
      status = currentLang === 'fr' ? 'Éligible QFZP' : 'QFZP eligible';
      sub = currentLang === 'fr' ? 'Vous semblez remplir les conditions' : 'You appear to meet the conditions';
    } else {
      head.className = 'dft-result-header warning';
      status = currentLang === 'fr' ? 'À sécuriser' : 'Needs review';
      sub = currentLang === 'fr' ? 'Certains critères nécessitent des ajustements' : 'Some criteria need adjustments';
    }
    $('dftResStatus').textContent = status;
    $('dftResScore').textContent = sub + ' · ' + (currentLang === 'fr' ? 'Score : ' : 'Score: ') + Math.round(pct) + '%';
    $('dftCriteriaList').innerHTML = qs.map(function(q, i){
      var a = answers[i];
      var ok = a !== undefined && !q.elim[a] && q.w[a] >= 2;
      return '<div class="dft-criteria-row"><div class="dft-criteria-icon ' + (ok ? 'ok' : 'ko') + '">' + (ok ? '✓' : '✕') + '</div><div>' + escapeHtml(q.q) + '</div></div>';
    }).join('');
  }


  function restart(){
    cur = 0;
    answers = [];
    $('dftQuizContainer').style.display = 'block';
    $('dftResultContainer').style.display = 'none';
    renderQ();
  }


  // Lang buttons
  root.querySelectorAll('.dft-lang-btn').forEach(function(b){
    b.addEventListener('click', function(){ setLang(b.getAttribute('data-lang')); });
  });


  // Prev / Restart
  $('dftPrevBtn').addEventListener('click', prev);
  $('dftRestartBtn').addEventListener('click', restart);


  // Init
  setLang(currentLang);
})();
</script>

        <div class="dft-form-group" id="dftPartGroup" style="display:none"><label class="dft-form-label" data-fr="Heures travaillées / semaine" data-en="Hours worked / week">Heures travaillées / semaine</label><input type="number" class="dft-form-input" id="dftPartHours" value="24" /></div>
      </div>

  <section class="dft-seo">
    <div class="dft-lang-fr">
      <h2>La <span>Gratuity</span> aux Émirats Arabes Unis</h2>
      <p>L'indemnité de fin de service (EOSB ou Gratuity) est régie par la loi fédérale sur le travail (Federal Decree-Law No. 33 of 2021, Article 51). Elle se calcule exclusivement sur le salaire de base (hors allowances).</p>
      <h3>Barème légal</h3>
      <ul><li><strong>Années 1 à 5</strong> : 21 jours de salaire par année d'ancienneté</li><li><strong>Au-delà de 5 ans</strong> : 30 jours par année supplémentaire</li><li><strong>Plafond</strong> : 2 ans de salaire maximum</li></ul>
      <h3>Cas particuliers</h3>
      <ul><li>Moins d'1 an : pas de gratuity</li><li>Entre 1 et 5 ans, démission sous ancien régime (pré-feb 2022) : réduction progressive</li><li>Licenciement pour faute grave Art. 44 : perte totale de la gratuity</li><li>Temps partiel : prorata au ratio heures travaillées / temps plein standard</li></ul>
      <h3>FAQ</h3>
      <div class="dft-faq-item"><div class="dft-faq-q">Quel salaire pris en compte pour la gratuity ?<span>+</span></div><div class="dft-faq-a">Uniquement le salaire de base (basic). Les allowances (housing, transport, etc.) sont exclues sauf si qualifiées contractuellement comme partie intégrante du salaire.</div></div>
      <div class="dft-faq-item"><div class="dft-faq-q">Dans quel délai l'employeur doit-il payer ?<span>+</span></div><div class="dft-faq-a">14 jours après la fin du contrat (Art. 53 de la loi). À défaut, pénalités de retard applicables devant le MOHRE.</div></div>
    </div>
    <div class="dft-lang-en">
      <h2>UAE <span>Gratuity</span> (End of Service Benefit)</h2>
      <p>End of Service Benefit (EOSB or Gratuity) is governed by the UAE Labour Law (Federal Decree-Law No. 33 of 2021, Article 51). It is calculated exclusively on the basic salary (excluding allowances).</p>
      <h3>Legal schedule</h3>
      <ul><li><strong>Years 1 to 5</strong>: 21 days of salary per year of service</li><li><strong>Beyond 5 years</strong>: 30 days per additional year</li><li><strong>Cap</strong>: maximum 2 years of salary</li></ul>
      <h3>Special cases</h3>
      <ul><li>Less than 1 year: no gratuity</li><li>Between 1 and 5 years, legacy regime resignation (pre-Feb 2022): progressive reduction</li><li>Termination for cause (Art. 44): total loss of gratuity</li><li>Part-time: prorated based on hours worked / full-time standard</li></ul>
      <h3>FAQ</h3>
      <div class="dft-faq-item"><div class="dft-faq-q">Which salary is used for gratuity?<span>+</span></div><div class="dft-faq-a">Basic salary only. Allowances (housing, transport, etc.) are excluded unless contractually qualified as an integral part of salary.</div></div>
      <div class="dft-faq-item"><div class="dft-faq-q">What's the payment deadline?<span>+</span></div><div class="dft-faq-a">14 days after contract end (Article 53). Late payment penalties applicable before MOHRE.</div></div>
    </div>
  </section>

<script>
(function(){
  var root = document.getElementById('dftGratCalc');
  if(!root) return;


  var currentLang = 'fr';


  try {
    var saved = localStorage.getItem('daftime_lang');
    if(saved) currentLang = saved;
    else if(navigator.language && navigator.language.indexOf('en')===0) currentLang = 'en';
  } catch(e){}


  function $(id){ return document.getElementById(id); }
  function n(id){ return parseFloat($(id).value) || 0; }
  function fmt(v){ return Math.round(v).toLocaleString(currentLang === 'en' ? 'en-US' : 'fr-FR'); }


  function setLang(l){
    currentLang = l;
    root.setAttribute('data-lang', l);
    try { localStorage.setItem('daftime_lang', l); } catch(e){}
    root.querySelectorAll('[data-fr]').forEach(function(el){
      var v = el.getAttribute('data-'+l);
      if(v !== null) el.innerHTML = v;
    });
    root.querySelectorAll('.dft-lang-btn').forEach(function(b){
      b.classList.toggle('active', b.getAttribute('data-lang') === l);
    });
    compute();
  }


  function compute(){
    var basic = n('dftBasic');
    var start = $('dftStartDate').value;
    var end = $('dftEndDate').value;
    var reason = $('dftReason').value;
    var ctype = $('dftCtype').value;
    var partH = n('dftPartHours');
    var l = currentLang;


    if(!start || !end){
      $('dftResMain').textContent = 'AED 0';
      $('dftResSub').textContent = '';
      $('dftBreakdown').innerHTML = '';
      $('dftTierVisual').innerHTML = '';
      return;
    }


    var startD = new Date(start);
    var endD = new Date(end);
    var years = (endD - startD) / (1000 * 60 * 60 * 24 * 365.25);
    if(years < 0) years = 0;


    var gratuity = 0, days = 0;
    if(reason === 'cause'){
      gratuity = 0;
    } else if(years < 1){
      gratuity = 0;
    } else {
      var dailyBasic = basic / 30;
      var y1_5 = Math.min(years, 5);
      var y5plus = Math.max(years - 5, 0);
      days = y1_5 * 21 + y5plus * 30;
      gratuity = days * dailyBasic;
      var cap = basic * 24;
      if(gratuity > cap) gratuity = cap;
    }
    if(ctype === 'part' && partH > 0){
      gratuity = gratuity * (partH / 48);
    }


    $('dftResMain').textContent = 'AED ' + fmt(gratuity);


    var sub = '';
    if(years < 1) sub = l === 'fr' ? '< 1 an : pas de gratuity' : '< 1 year: no gratuity';
    else if(reason === 'cause') sub = l === 'fr' ? 'Faute grave Art. 44 : gratuity perdue' : 'Cause termination Art. 44: gratuity forfeited';
    else sub = years.toFixed(2) + (l === 'fr' ? ' ans d\'ancienneté · ' : ' years of service · ') + Math.round(days) + (l === 'fr' ? ' jours' : ' days');
    $('dftResSub').textContent = sub;


    var tier1Active = years >= 1 && years <= 5;
    var tier2Active = years > 5;
    $('dftTierVisual').innerHTML =
      '<div class="dft-tier' + (tier1Active ? ' active' : '') + '"><div class="dft-tier-years">1-5 ' + (l === 'fr' ? 'ans' : 'yrs') + '</div><div class="dft-tier-desc">' + (l === 'fr' ? '21 jours de salaire / an' : '21 days / year') + '</div><div class="dft-tier-days">21 ' + (l === 'fr' ? 'j' : 'd') + '</div></div>' +
      '<div class="dft-tier' + (tier2Active ? ' active' : '') + '"><div class="dft-tier-years">5+ ' + (l === 'fr' ? 'ans' : 'yrs') + '</div><div class="dft-tier-desc">' + (l === 'fr' ? '30 jours / an supplémentaire' : '30 days / additional year') + '</div><div class="dft-tier-days">30 ' + (l === 'fr' ? 'j' : 'd') + '</div></div>' +
      '<div class="dft-tier"><div class="dft-tier-years">Cap</div><div class="dft-tier-desc">' + (l === 'fr' ? 'Plafond : 2 ans de salaire' : 'Cap: 2 years of salary') + '</div><div class="dft-tier-days">24 ' + (l === 'fr' ? 'mois' : 'm') + '</div></div>';


    $('dftBreakdown').innerHTML =
      '<div class="dft-result-row"><span>' + (l === 'fr' ? 'Salaire de base' : 'Basic salary') + '</span><span class="dft-val">AED ' + fmt(basic) + '</span></div>' +
      '<div class="dft-result-row"><span>' + (l === 'fr' ? 'Ancienneté' : 'Service') + '</span><span class="dft-val">' + years.toFixed(2) + ' ' + (l === 'fr' ? 'ans' : 'yrs') + '</span></div>' +
      '<div class="dft-result-row"><span>' + (l === 'fr' ? 'Jours de gratuity' : 'Gratuity days') + '</span><span class="dft-val">' + Math.round(days) + '</span></div>' +
      '<div class="dft-result-row dft-highlight"><span>GRATUITY</span><span class="dft-val">AED ' + fmt(gratuity) + '</span></div>';
  }


  // Show/hide part-time hours field
  $('dftCtype').addEventListener('change', function(){
    $('dftPartGroup').style.display = this.value === 'part' ? 'flex' : 'none';
    compute();
  });


  // Lang buttons
  root.querySelectorAll('.dft-lang-btn').forEach(function(b){
    b.addEventListener('click', function(){ setLang(b.getAttribute('data-lang')); });
  });


  // FAQ
  root.querySelectorAll('.dft-faq-item').forEach(function(item){
    item.addEventListener('click', function(){ item.classList.toggle('open'); });
  });


  // Live compute
  ['dftBasic','dftStartDate','dftEndDate','dftReason','dftCtype','dftPartHours'].forEach(function(id){
    var el = $(id);
    el.addEventListener('input', compute);
    el.addEventListener('change', compute);
  });


  // Default dates: today and 2 years ago
  var today = new Date();
  var twoYrsAgo = new Date(); twoYrsAgo.setFullYear(today.getFullYear() - 2);
  $('dftStartDate').valueAsDate = twoYrsAgo;
  $('dftEndDate').valueAsDate = today;


  setLang(currentLang);
})();
</script>

  <section class="dft-seo">
    <div class="dft-lang-fr">
      <h2>Coût réel d'un <span>employé</span> aux Émirats</h2>
      <p>Aux UAE, pas de cotisations sociales employeur (sauf DEWS à Dubai pour certains types de contrats ou pension des nationaux). Le coût total comprend : salaire brut + allowances + visa amorti + assurance santé obligatoire + billet annuel + provision gratuity.</p>
      <h3>Composition d'un salary package UAE</h3>
      <ul><li><strong>Basic salary</strong> : 50-60% du package (base de calcul gratuity)</li><li><strong>Housing allowance</strong> : 20-25% du package</li><li><strong>Transport allowance</strong> : 5-10% du package</li><li><strong>Other allowances</strong> : éducation, téléphone, etc.</li></ul>
      <h3>Charges récurrentes employeur</h3>
      <ul><li>Visa de travail : ~AED 5 000-8 000 pour 2 ans</li><li>Emirates ID : AED 370 pour 2 ans</li><li>Assurance santé : AED 2 000 à 8 000 / an selon niveau</li><li>Medical fitness test : AED 350</li><li>Gratuity : provision ~8,3% du basic pour les 5 premières années</li></ul>
      <h3>FAQ</h3>
      <div class="dft-faq-item"><div class="dft-faq-q">Y a-t-il des cotisations sociales ?<span>+</span></div><div class="dft-faq-a">Pour les expatriés : non. Pour les nationaux UAE/GCC : GPSSA (pension publique) ~20% (12,5% employeur / 5% employé / 2,5% État). À Dubai, certaines sociétés opt-in au DEWS qui remplace la gratuity par des versements mensuels ~5,83%.</div></div>
      <div class="dft-faq-item"><div class="dft-faq-q">Quelle provision gratuity comptabiliser ?<span>+</span></div><div class="dft-faq-a">21 jours de basic par année d'ancienneté les 5 premières années → ~5,83% mensuel. Puis 30 jours par année → ~8,33% mensuel. Comptabiliser en charges à payer au bilan.</div></div>
    </div>
    <div class="dft-lang-en">
      <h2>True <span>employee</span> cost in the UAE</h2>
      <p>In the UAE, there are no employer social charges (except DEWS in Dubai for some contracts or pensions for nationals). Total cost includes: gross salary + allowances + amortised visa + mandatory medical insurance + annual flight + gratuity accrual.</p>
      <h3>Typical UAE salary package composition</h3>
      <ul><li><strong>Basic salary</strong>: 50-60% of package (gratuity base)</li><li><strong>Housing allowance</strong>: 20-25% of package</li><li><strong>Transport allowance</strong>: 5-10% of package</li><li><strong>Other allowances</strong>: education, phone, etc.</li></ul>
      <h3>Recurring employer costs</h3>
      <ul><li>Work visa: ~AED 5,000-8,000 for 2 years</li><li>Emirates ID: AED 370 for 2 years</li><li>Medical insurance: AED 2,000 to 8,000 / year depending on level</li><li>Medical fitness test: AED 350</li><li>Gratuity: ~8.3% accrual on basic for the first 5 years</li></ul>
      <h3>FAQ</h3>
      <div class="dft-faq-item"><div class="dft-faq-q">Are there social charges?<span>+</span></div><div class="dft-faq-a">For expatriates: no. For UAE/GCC nationals: GPSSA (public pension) ~20% (12.5% employer / 5% employee / 2.5% State). In Dubai, some companies opt in to DEWS which replaces gratuity with monthly contributions ~5.83%.</div></div>
      <div class="dft-faq-item"><div class="dft-faq-q">What gratuity provision should I book?<span>+</span></div><div class="dft-faq-a">21 days of basic per year of service for the first 5 years → ~5.83% monthly. Then 30 days per year → ~8.33% monthly. Record as accrued charges on the balance sheet.</div></div>
    </div>
  </section>

<script>
(function(){
  var root = document.getElementById('dftEmpCost');
  if(!root) return;


  // Force English by default on this tool, ignore any saved preference
  var currentLang = 'en';


  function $(id){ return document.getElementById(id); }
  function n(id){ return parseFloat($(id).value) || 0; }
  function fmt(v){ return Math.round(v).toLocaleString(currentLang === 'en' ? 'en-US' : 'fr-FR'); }


  function setLang(l){
    currentLang = l;
    root.setAttribute('data-lang', l);
    root.querySelectorAll('[data-fr]').forEach(function(el){
      var v = el.getAttribute('data-'+l);
      if(v !== null) el.innerHTML = v;
    });
    root.querySelectorAll('.dft-lang-btn').forEach(function(b){
      b.classList.toggle('active', b.getAttribute('data-lang') === l);
    });
    compute();
  }


  function compute(){
    var basic = n('dftBasic') * 12;
    var housing = n('dftHousing') * 12;
    var transport = n('dftTransport') * 12;
    var bonus = n('dftBonus');
    var medical = n('dftMedical');
    var visa = n('dftVisa') / 2;
    var ticket = $('dftTicket').checked ? 3000 : 0;
    var recruit = $('dftRecruit').checked ? n('dftBasic') : 0;
    var gratuity = basic * 0.0583;
    var total = basic + housing + transport + bonus + medical + visa + ticket + recruit + gratuity;
    var l = currentLang;


    $('dftResMain').textContent = 'AED ' + fmt(total);
    $('dftResSub').textContent = (l === 'fr' ? 'Soit ' : 'About ') + fmt(total / 12) + (l === 'fr' ? ' AED / mois tout compris' : ' AED / month all-in');


    function pct(v){ return total > 0 ? (v / total * 100).toFixed(1) : 0; }


    $('dftBarViz').innerHTML =
      '<div class="dft-bar-seg basic" style="width:' + pct(basic) + '%">' + (pct(basic) >= 8 ? pct(basic) + '%' : '') + '</div>' +
      '<div class="dft-bar-seg allowances" style="width:' + pct(housing+transport+bonus) + '%">' + (pct(housing+transport+bonus) >= 8 ? pct(housing+transport+bonus) + '%' : '') + '</div>' +
      '<div class="dft-bar-seg insurance" style="width:' + pct(medical+ticket) + '%">' + (pct(medical+ticket) >= 8 ? pct(medical+ticket) + '%' : '') + '</div>' +
      '<div class="dft-bar-seg visa" style="width:' + pct(visa+recruit) + '%">' + (pct(visa+recruit) >= 8 ? pct(visa+recruit) + '%' : '') + '</div>' +
      '<div class="dft-bar-seg gratuity" style="width:' + pct(gratuity) + '%">' + (pct(gratuity) >= 8 ? pct(gratuity) + '%' : '') + '</div>';


    var labBasic = 'Basic';
    var labAllow = l === 'fr' ? 'Allowances' : 'Allowances';
    var labBenef = l === 'fr' ? 'Avantages' : 'Benefits';
    var labVisa = l === 'fr' ? 'Visa / Recrutement' : 'Visa / Recruitment';
    var labGrat = l === 'fr' ? 'Provision EOSB' : 'EOSB accrual';


    $('dftBreakdown').innerHTML =
      '<div class="dft-legend">' +
        '<div class="dft-legend-item"><div class="dft-legend-color" style="background:#1a1d56"></div>' + labBasic + '</div>' +
        '<div class="dft-legend-item"><div class="dft-legend-color" style="background:#2a3e8f"></div>' + labAllow + '</div>' +
        '<div class="dft-legend-item"><div class="dft-legend-color" style="background:#d4af37"></div>' + labBenef + '</div>' +
        '<div class="dft-legend-item"><div class="dft-legend-color" style="background:#a08028"></div>' + labVisa + '</div>' +
        '<div class="dft-legend-item"><div class="dft-legend-color" style="background:#6b5820"></div>' + labGrat + '</div>' +
      '</div>' +
      '<div class="dft-result-row"><span>' + labBasic + '</span><span class="dft-val">' + fmt(basic) + '</span></div>' +
      '<div class="dft-result-row"><span>' + (l === 'fr' ? 'Logement + transport + bonus' : 'Housing + transport + bonus') + '</span><span class="dft-val">' + fmt(housing + transport + bonus) + '</span></div>' +
      '<div class="dft-result-row"><span>' + (l === 'fr' ? 'Assurance + billet' : 'Insurance + flight') + '</span><span class="dft-val">' + fmt(medical + ticket) + '</span></div>' +
      '<div class="dft-result-row"><span>' + labVisa + '</span><span class="dft-val">' + fmt(visa + recruit) + '</span></div>' +
      '<div class="dft-result-row"><span>' + labGrat + '</span><span class="dft-val">' + fmt(gratuity) + '</span></div>' +
      '<div class="dft-result-row dft-highlight"><span>' + (l === 'fr' ? 'TOTAL / AN' : 'TOTAL / YEAR') + '</span><span class="dft-val">AED ' + fmt(total) + '</span></div>';
  }


  // Lang buttons
  root.querySelectorAll('.dft-lang-btn').forEach(function(b){
    b.addEventListener('click', function(){ setLang(b.getAttribute('data-lang')); });
  });


  // FAQ
  root.querySelectorAll('.dft-faq-item').forEach(function(item){
    item.addEventListener('click', function(){ item.classList.toggle('open'); });
  });


  // Live compute
  ['dftBasic','dftHousing','dftTransport','dftBonus','dftMedical','dftVisa','dftTicket','dftRecruit'].forEach(function(id){
    var el = $(id);
    el.addEventListener('input', compute);
    el.addEventListener('change', compute);
  });


  setLang(currentLang);
})();
</script>

    <div class="dft-lang-fr">
      <h2>Investir dans l'<span>immobilier Dubai</span> en 2026</h2>
      <p>Dubai offre l'un des rendements locatifs les plus attractifs au monde : 5 à 8% brut. Les frais d'acquisition restent modérés (~6-8%) et la fiscalité est nulle (pas d'IR, pas de taxe foncière, pas de plus-value).</p>
      <h3>Frais d'acquisition (one-off)</h3>
      <ul><li><strong>DLD (Dubai Land Department)</strong> : 4% du prix + AED 540 admin</li><li><strong>Agent immobilier</strong> : 2% + VAT</li><li><strong>Trustee office</strong> : AED 4 000 à 6 500</li><li><strong>NOC développeur</strong> (secondary uniquement) : AED 500 à 5 000</li><li><strong>Mortgage fees</strong> si financement : ~0,25% + registration</li></ul>
      <h3>Charges récurrentes</h3>
      <ul><li>Service charges : AED 10-25 / sqft / an selon tour</li><li>DEWA et chiller : variable (souvent payé par le locataire)</li><li>Insurance : AED 500-1 500 / an</li><li>Management fee : 5-8% du loyer annuel</li></ul>
      <h3>FAQ</h3>
      <div class="dft-faq-item"><div class="dft-faq-q">L'investissement Dubai est-il halal ?<span>+</span></div><div class="dft-faq-a">Un achat en cash est conforme à la Sharia. Pour un financement, privilégier une banque islamique (Dubai Islamic Bank, ADIB, Emirates Islamic) avec un contrat Ijara ou Murabaha plutôt qu'un prêt classique à intérêt.</div></div>
      <div class="dft-faq-item"><div class="dft-faq-q">Quel visa l'immobilier permet-il d'obtenir ?<span>+</span></div><div class="dft-faq-a">Investment visa 2 ans dès AED 750 000, Golden Visa 10 ans dès AED 2M. Le bien doit être ready (pas off-plan) et financé à plus de 50% en fonds propres.</div></div>
    </div>
    <div class="dft-lang-en">
      <h2>Investing in <span>Dubai real estate</span> in 2026</h2>
      <p>Dubai offers one of the world's most attractive rental yields: 5 to 8% gross. Acquisition costs remain moderate (~6-8%) and taxation is nil (no income tax, no property tax, no capital gains tax).</p>
      <h3>One-off acquisition costs</h3>
      <ul><li><strong>DLD (Dubai Land Department)</strong>: 4% of price + AED 540 admin</li><li><strong>Real estate agent</strong>: 2% + VAT</li><li><strong>Trustee office</strong>: AED 4,000 to 6,500</li><li><strong>Developer NOC</strong> (secondary only): AED 500 to 5,000</li><li><strong>Mortgage fees</strong> if financed: ~0.25% + registration</li></ul>
      <h3>Recurring charges</h3>
      <ul><li>Service charges: AED 10-25 / sqft / year depending on tower</li><li>DEWA and chiller: variable (often paid by tenant)</li><li>Insurance: AED 500-1,500 / year</li><li>Management fee: 5-8% of annual rent</li></ul>
      <h3>FAQ</h3>
      <div class="dft-faq-item"><div class="dft-faq-q">Is Dubai property halal-compliant?<span>+</span></div><div class="dft-faq-a">Cash purchases are Sharia-compliant. For financing, prefer an Islamic bank (Dubai Islamic Bank, ADIB, Emirates Islamic) with an Ijara or Murabaha contract rather than a conventional interest-bearing loan.</div></div>
      <div class="dft-faq-item"><div class="dft-faq-q">What visa can real estate provide?<span>+</span></div><div class="dft-faq-a">Investment visa 2 years from AED 750,000; Golden Visa 10 years from AED 2M. Property must be ready (not off-plan) and over 50% equity-financed.</div></div>
    </div>

<script>
(function(){
  var root = document.getElementById('dftRoiDxb');
  if(!root) return;


  // Force English by default, ignore any saved preference
  var currentLang = 'en';


  function $(id){ return document.getElementById(id); }
  function n(id){ return parseFloat($(id).value) || 0; }
  function fmt(v){ return Math.round(v).toLocaleString(currentLang === 'en' ? 'en-US' : 'fr-FR'); }
  function escapeHtml(s){
    return String(s).replace(/[&<>"']/g, function(c){
      return {'&':'&amp;','<':'&lt;','>':'&gt;','"':'&quot;',"'":'&#39;'}[c];
    });
  }


  var yields = {jvc:7.2, marina:6.0, downtown:5.5, business:6.5, jlt:6.8, palm:5.0, other:null};


  function setLang(l){
    currentLang = l;
    root.setAttribute('data-lang', l);
    root.querySelectorAll('[data-fr]').forEach(function(el){
      var v = el.getAttribute('data-'+l);
      if(v !== null) el.innerHTML = v;
    });
    root.querySelectorAll('.dft-lang-btn').forEach(function(b){
      b.classList.toggle('active', b.getAttribute('data-lang') === l);
    });
    compute();
  }


  function compute(){
    var price = n('dftPrice');
    var sqft = n('dftSqft');
    var ptype = $('dftPtype').value;
    var gross = n('dftGrossYield') / 100;
    var svc = n('dftSvcCharge') * sqft;
    var vac = n('dftVacancy') / 100;
    var mgmt = n('dftMgmt') / 100;
    var maint = n('dftMaint') / 100;
    var l = currentLang;


    // Acquisition costs
    var dld = price * 0.04 + 540;
    var agent = price * 0.02 * 1.05;
    var trustee = 6500;
    var noc = ptype === 'ready' ? 2500 : 0;
    var totalAcq = price + dld + agent + trustee + noc;


    // Rental
    var grossRent = price * gross;
    var effectiveRent = grossRent * (1 - vac);
    var mgmtFee = effectiveRent * mgmt;
    var maintFee = price * maint;
    var netRent = effectiveRent - svc - mgmtFee - maintFee;
    var netYield = totalAcq > 0 ? netRent / totalAcq * 100 : 0;
    var payback = netRent > 0 ? totalAcq / netRent : 0;


    $('dftResYield').textContent = netYield.toFixed(2) + '%';
    $('dftResSub').textContent = (l === 'fr' ? 'Payback net : ' : 'Net payback: ') +
      (payback > 0 ? payback.toFixed(1) + (l === 'fr' ? ' ans' : ' years') : 'N/A');


    var labels = l === 'fr' ? {
      acq:'ACQUISITION', price:"Prix d'achat", dld:'DLD (4% + 540)', agent:'Agent (2% + VAT)', trustee:'Trustee office', noc:'NOC', totalAcq:'Total investissement',
      rent:'EXPLOITATION ANNUELLE', grossRent:'Loyer brut théorique', vac:'Vacance', effRent:'Loyer effectif', svc:'Service charges', mgmt:'Gestion', maint:'Maintenance', netRent:'Revenu net annuel',
      halal:'Rappel : achat cash = halal. Pour financement, privilégier Dubai Islamic Bank, ADIB ou Emirates Islamic (Ijara/Murabaha)'
    } : {
      acq:'ACQUISITION', price:'Purchase price', dld:'DLD (4% + 540)', agent:'Agent (2% + VAT)', trustee:'Trustee office', noc:'NOC', totalAcq:'Total investment',
      rent:'ANNUAL OPERATION', grossRent:'Gross theoretical rent', vac:'Vacancy', effRent:'Effective rent', svc:'Service charges', mgmt:'Management', maint:'Maintenance', netRent:'Net annual income',
      halal:'Reminder: cash purchase = halal. For financing, prefer Dubai Islamic Bank, ADIB or Emirates Islamic (Ijara/Murabaha)'
    };


    var html = '<h4>' + labels.acq + '</h4>' +
      '<div class="dft-result-row"><span>' + labels.price + '</span><span class="dft-val">' + fmt(price) + '</span></div>' +
      '<div class="dft-result-row"><span>' + labels.dld + '</span><span class="dft-val">' + fmt(dld) + '</span></div>' +
      '<div class="dft-result-row"><span>' + labels.agent + '</span><span class="dft-val">' + fmt(agent) + '</span></div>' +
      '<div class="dft-result-row"><span>' + labels.trustee + '</span><span class="dft-val">' + fmt(trustee) + '</span></div>' +
      (noc > 0 ? '<div class="dft-result-row"><span>' + labels.noc + '</span><span class="dft-val">' + fmt(noc) + '</span></div>' : '') +
      '<div class="dft-result-row dft-highlight"><span>' + labels.totalAcq + '</span><span class="dft-val">' + fmt(totalAcq) + '</span></div>' +
      '<h4 class="dft-h-spaced">' + labels.rent + '</h4>' +
      '<div class="dft-result-row"><span>' + labels.grossRent + '</span><span class="dft-val">+' + fmt(grossRent) + '</span></div>' +
      '<div class="dft-result-row"><span>' + labels.vac + ' (-' + n('dftVacancy') + '%)</span><span class="dft-val">-' + fmt(grossRent * vac) + '</span></div>' +
      '<div class="dft-result-row"><span>' + labels.svc + '</span><span class="dft-val">-' + fmt(svc) + '</span></div>' +
      '<div class="dft-result-row"><span>' + labels.mgmt + '</span><span class="dft-val">-' + fmt(mgmtFee) + '</span></div>' +
      '<div class="dft-result-row"><span>' + labels.maint + '</span><span class="dft-val">-' + fmt(maintFee) + '</span></div>' +
      '<div class="dft-result-row dft-highlight"><span>' + labels.netRent + '</span><span class="dft-val">AED ' + fmt(netRent) + '</span></div>' +
      '<div class="dft-alert success"><span class="dft-alert-icon">✓</span><div>' + labels.halal + '</div></div>';


    $('dftBreakdown').innerHTML = html;
  }


  // Zone change → auto-fill gross yield
  $('dftZone').addEventListener('change', function(){
    var y = yields[this.value];
    if(y !== null && y !== undefined) $('dftGrossYield').value = y;
    compute();
  });


  // Lang buttons
  root.querySelectorAll('.dft-lang-btn').forEach(function(b){
    b.addEventListener('click', function(){ setLang(b.getAttribute('data-lang')); });
  });


  // FAQ
  root.querySelectorAll('.dft-faq-item').forEach(function(item){
    item.addEventListener('click', function(){ item.classList.toggle('open'); });
  });


  // Live compute on all inputs
  ['dftPrice','dftSqft','dftPtype','dftGrossYield','dftSvcCharge','dftVacancy','dftMgmt','dftMaint'].forEach(function(id){
    var el = $(id);
    el.addEventListener('input', compute);
    el.addEventListener('change', compute);
  });


  setLang(currentLang);
})();
</script>

  <section class="dft-seo">
    <div class="dft-lang-fr">
      <h2>Régime des <span>pénalités FTA</span> aux UAE</h2>
      <p>Le Cabinet Decision No. 40 of 2017 (modifié par No. 49 of 2021) pour la VAT et le Cabinet Decision No. 75 of 2023 pour la Corporate Tax fixent les pénalités FTA. Les montants peuvent atteindre plusieurs fois la taxe due.</p>
      <h3>Pénalités VAT principales</h3>
      <ul><li>Défaut d'enregistrement : AED 10 000</li><li>Retard de déclaration : AED 1 000 (1re), AED 2 000 (récidive)</li><li>Retard de paiement : 2% immédiat + 4% après 7 jours + 1% par jour (plafond 300%)</li><li>Défaut de désenregistrement : AED 1 000 / mois (plafond 10 000)</li></ul>
      <h3>Pénalités Corporate Tax principales</h3>
      <ul><li>Défaut d'enregistrement : AED 10 000</li><li>Retard de déclaration : AED 500 / mois (0-12 mois) puis AED 1 000 / mois</li><li>Retard de paiement : 14% par an sur le montant dû</li><li>Déclaration incorrecte : 1 à 25% de la taxe éludée selon bonne foi</li></ul>
      <h3>Voluntary Disclosure</h3>
      <p>Si vous identifiez une erreur avant un contrôle FTA, déposez une Voluntary Disclosure (Form 211 pour VAT, équivalent pour CT). Réduction substantielle des pénalités.</p>
    </div>
    <div class="dft-lang-en">
      <h2><span>FTA penalty</span> regime in the UAE</h2>
      <p>Cabinet Decision No. 40 of 2017 (as amended by No. 49 of 2021) for VAT and Cabinet Decision No. 75 of 2023 for Corporate Tax set out the FTA penalties. Amounts can reach several multiples of the tax due.</p>
      <h3>Key VAT penalties</h3>
      <ul><li>Late registration: AED 10,000</li><li>Late filing: AED 1,000 (first), AED 2,000 (repeat)</li><li>Late payment: 2% immediately + 4% after 7 days + 1% per day (capped 300%)</li><li>Late deregistration: AED 1,000 / month (capped 10,000)</li></ul>
      <h3>Key Corporate Tax penalties</h3>
      <ul><li>Late registration: AED 10,000</li><li>Late filing: AED 500 / month (0-12 months) then AED 1,000 / month</li><li>Late payment: 14% annual on tax due</li><li>Incorrect return: 1 to 25% of evaded tax depending on good faith</li></ul>
      <h3>Voluntary Disclosure</h3>
      <p>If you detect an error before an FTA audit, file a Voluntary Disclosure (Form 211 for VAT, equivalent for CT). Substantial penalty reduction.</p>
    </div>
  </section>


  <div class="dft-cta">
    <h3 data-fr='Réduisez vos <span>pénalités FTA</span>' data-en='Reduce your <span>FTA penalties</span>'>Reduce your <span>FTA penalties</span></h3>
    <p data-fr="Voluntary disclosure, réclamations, contentieux : nos experts FTA-registered négocient vos amendes." data-en="Voluntary disclosure, claims, disputes: our FTA-registered experts negotiate your penalties.">Voluntary disclosure, claims, disputes: our FTA-registered experts negotiate your penalties.</p>
    <a href="https://daftime.ae/contact" target="_blank" rel="noopener" class="dft-btn" data-fr="Prendre rendez-vous" data-en="Book a meeting">Book a meeting</a>
  </div>

<script>
(function(){
  var root = document.getElementById('dftFtaPen');
  if(!root) return;


  // Force English by default, ignore any saved preference
  var currentLang = 'en';
  var currentTax = 'vat';


  function $(id){ return document.getElementById(id); }
  function fmt(v){ return Math.round(v).toLocaleString(currentLang === 'en' ? 'en-US' : 'fr-FR'); }
  function escapeHtml(s){
    return String(s).replace(/[&<>"']/g, function(c){
      return {'&':'&amp;','<':'&lt;','>':'&gt;','"':'&quot;',"'":'&#39;'}[c];
    });
  }


  var penalties = {
    vat: [
      {id:'late_reg', fr:"Défaut d'enregistrement VAT", en:'Late VAT registration', type:'fixed', v:10000, desc:{fr:'Montant fixe AED 10 000', en:'Fixed AED 10,000'}},
      {id:'late_filing', fr:'Retard de déclaration', en:'Late return filing', type:'fixed', v:1000, desc:{fr:'AED 1 000 (1re) / 2 000 (récidive)', en:'AED 1,000 (first) / 2,000 (repeat)'}},
      {id:'late_payment', fr:'Retard de paiement', en:'Late payment', type:'progressive', desc:{fr:'2% + 4% après 7j + 1% / jour (cap 300%)', en:'2% + 4% after 7d + 1% / day (cap 300%)'}},
      {id:'no_dereg', fr:'Défaut de désenregistrement', en:'Late deregistration', type:'monthly_cap', v:1000, cap:10000, desc:{fr:'AED 1 000 / mois (cap 10 000)', en:'AED 1,000 / month (cap 10,000)'}}
    ],
    ct: [
      {id:'late_reg_ct', fr:"Défaut d'enregistrement CT", en:'Late CT registration', type:'fixed', v:10000, desc:{fr:'Montant fixe AED 10 000', en:'Fixed AED 10,000'}},
      {id:'late_filing_ct', fr:'Retard de déclaration CT', en:'Late CT filing', type:'monthly_tier', v1:500, v2:1000, tier:12, desc:{fr:'AED 500/mois (0-12) puis 1 000/mois', en:'AED 500/month (0-12) then 1,000/month'}},
      {id:'late_payment_ct', fr:'Retard de paiement CT', en:'Late CT payment', type:'annual_pct', pct:0.14, desc:{fr:'14% par an sur montant dû', en:'14% per year on amount due'}}
    ]
  };


  // Track which penalties are checked across tab switches
  var checkedIds = {};


  function setLang(l){
    currentLang = l;
    root.setAttribute('data-lang', l);
    root.querySelectorAll('[data-fr]').forEach(function(el){
      var v = el.getAttribute('data-'+l);
      if(v !== null) el.innerHTML = v;
    });
    root.querySelectorAll('.dft-lang-btn').forEach(function(b){
      b.classList.toggle('active', b.getAttribute('data-lang') === l);
    });
    renderList();
    compute();
  }


  function renderList(){
    var list = penalties[currentTax];
    var html = list.map(function(p){
      var label = currentLang === 'en' ? p.en : p.fr;
      var desc = currentLang === 'en' ? p.desc.en : p.desc.fr;
      var checked = checkedIds[p.id] ? ' checked' : '';
      return '<label class="dft-penalty-item">' +
        '<input type="checkbox" data-id="' + p.id + '"' + checked + '>' +
        '<div><div class="dft-penalty-label">' + escapeHtml(label) + '</div><div class="dft-penalty-desc">' + escapeHtml(desc) + '</div></div>' +
      '</label>';
    }).join('');
    $('dftPenaltyList').innerHTML = html;
    $('dftPenaltyList').querySelectorAll('input[data-id]').forEach(function(cb){
      cb.addEventListener('change', function(){
        checkedIds[cb.getAttribute('data-id')] = cb.checked;
        compute();
      });
    });
  }


  function compute(){
    var selected = [];
    $('dftPenaltyList').querySelectorAll('input:checked').forEach(function(cb){
      selected.push(cb.getAttribute('data-id'));
    });
    var tax = parseFloat($('dftTaxAmount').value) || 0;
    var days = parseFloat($('dftLateDays').value) || 0;
    var months = parseFloat($('dftLateMonths').value) || 0;
    var l = currentLang;


    var needsTax = selected.some(function(id){ return id === 'late_payment' || id === 'late_payment_ct'; });
    var needsDays = selected.some(function(id){ return id === 'late_payment'; });
    var needsMonths = selected.some(function(id){ return id === 'no_dereg' || id === 'late_filing_ct' || id === 'late_payment_ct'; });
    $('dftTaxAmountGroup').style.display = needsTax ? 'flex' : 'none';
    $('dftDaysGroup').style.display = needsDays ? 'flex' : 'none';
    $('dftMonthsGroup').style.display = needsMonths ? 'flex' : 'none';


    var total = 0, rows = [];
    selected.forEach(function(id){
      var p = null;
      for(var i = 0; i < penalties[currentTax].length; i++){
        if(penalties[currentTax][i].id === id){ p = penalties[currentTax][i]; break; }
      }
      if(!p) return;
      var amt = 0;
      if(p.type === 'fixed') amt = p.v;
      else if(p.type === 'monthly_cap') amt = Math.min(months * p.v, p.cap);
      else if(p.type === 'monthly_tier') amt = Math.min(months, p.tier) * p.v1 + Math.max(months - p.tier, 0) * p.v2;
      else if(p.type === 'annual_pct') amt = tax * p.pct * (months / 12);
      else if(p.type === 'progressive'){
        var pct = 0.02;
        if(days >= 7) pct += 0.04;
        if(days > 7) pct += (days - 7) * 0.01;
        if(pct > 3) pct = 3;
        amt = tax * pct;
      }
      total += amt;
      rows.push({k: l === 'en' ? p.en : p.fr, v: amt});
    });


    $('dftResMain').textContent = 'AED ' + fmt(total);
    $('dftResSub').textContent = selected.length + (l === 'fr' ? ' pénalité(s) sélectionnée(s)' : ' penalty(ies) selected');


    if(rows.length === 0){
      $('dftBreakdown').innerHTML = '<div class="dft-empty">' + (l === 'fr' ? 'Sélectionnez les pénalités applicables' : 'Select applicable penalties') + '</div>';
    } else {
      var html = rows.map(function(r){
        return '<div class="dft-result-row"><span>' + escapeHtml(r.k) + '</span><span class="dft-val">' + fmt(r.v) + '</span></div>';
      }).join('');
      html += '<div class="dft-result-row dft-highlight"><span>TOTAL</span><span class="dft-val">AED ' + fmt(total) + '</span></div>';
      html += '<div class="dft-alert"><span class="dft-alert-icon">ⓘ</span><div>' + (l === 'fr' ? 'Une Voluntary Disclosure (Form 211 VAT) peut réduire substantiellement ces pénalités. Contactez Daftime avant un contrôle FTA.' : 'A Voluntary Disclosure (Form 211 VAT) may substantially reduce these penalties. Contact Daftime before an FTA audit.') + '</div></div>';
      $('dftBreakdown').innerHTML = html;
    }
  }


  // Tabs
  root.querySelectorAll('.dft-tab').forEach(function(t){
    t.addEventListener('click', function(){
      root.querySelectorAll('.dft-tab').forEach(function(x){ x.classList.remove('active'); });
      t.classList.add('active');
      currentTax = t.getAttribute('data-tax');
      // Reset checked state when switching tax type (different penalty sets)
      checkedIds = {};
      renderList();
      compute();
    });
  });


  // Lang buttons
  root.querySelectorAll('.dft-lang-btn').forEach(function(b){
    b.addEventListener('click', function(){ setLang(b.getAttribute('data-lang')); });
  });


  // Conditional input fields recompute on change
  ['dftTaxAmount','dftLateDays','dftLateMonths'].forEach(function(id){
    var el = $(id);
    el.addEventListener('input', compute);
    el.addEventListener('change', compute);
  });


  setLang(currentLang);
})();
</script>
________________

  <section class="dft-seo">
    <div class="dft-lang-fr">
      <h2>Distribuer des <span>dividendes</span> depuis les UAE</h2>
      <p>Les UAE n'appliquent aucune retenue à la source (WHT) sur les dividendes sortants : 0%. L'imposition totale dépend donc de la résidence fiscale de l'actionnaire et des conventions fiscales (DTT).</p>
      <h3>Côté UAE</h3>
      <ul><li>Corporate Tax (0% ou 9%) au niveau de la société</li><li>Réserve légale : 10% du bénéfice net jusqu'à 50% du capital social</li><li>WHT sur dividendes sortants : 0%</li><li>Pas de taxe sur les plus-values</li></ul>
      <h3>Côté actionnaire (résidents fiscaux)</h3>
      <p>Particulier France : PFU 30% (12,8% IR + 17,2% prélèvements sociaux) ou barème progressif + CSG/CRDS. Particulier Belgique : précompte mobilier 30%. Luxembourg : exonération partielle 50% pour dividendes éligibles, puis tranche IR. Canada : imposition comme dividendes étrangers, crédit DTT.</p>
      <h3>FAQ</h3>
      <div class="dft-faq-item"><div class="dft-faq-q">Participation exemption pour holdings ?<span>+</span></div><div class="dft-faq-a">Oui. Si la société UAE détient ≥ 5% du capital d'une filiale pendant ≥ 12 mois et que la filiale est imposée à ≥ 9% (condition de substance équivalente), les dividendes reçus sont exonérés (Art. 22 du Federal Decree-Law No. 47 of 2022).</div></div>
      <div class="dft-faq-item"><div class="dft-faq-q">Les UAE ont-ils une convention fiscale avec la France ?<span>+</span></div><div class="dft-faq-a">Oui, convention du 19/07/1989. Les dividendes de source UAE sont imposables en France mais bénéficient d'un crédit d'impôt forfaitaire. Pour les résidents fiscaux UAE certifiés (TRC), exonération en France.</div></div>
    </div>
    <div class="dft-lang-en">
      <h2>Distributing <span>dividends</span> from the UAE</h2>
      <p>The UAE applies no withholding tax (WHT) on outbound dividends: 0%. Total taxation therefore depends on the shareholder's tax residence and applicable tax treaties (DTT).</p>
      <h3>UAE side</h3>
      <ul><li>Corporate Tax (0% or 9%) at company level</li><li>Legal reserve: 10% of net profit up to 50% of share capital</li><li>WHT on outbound dividends: 0%</li><li>No capital gains tax</li></ul>
      <h3>Shareholder side (tax residents)</h3>
      <p>French individual: PFU flat rate 30% (12.8% IT + 17.2% social contributions) or progressive scale + CSG/CRDS. Belgian individual: withholding 30%. Luxembourg: 50% partial exemption for qualifying dividends, then IT bracket. Canadian: foreign dividend taxation with DTT credit.</p>
      <h3>FAQ</h3>
      <div class="dft-faq-item"><div class="dft-faq-q">Participation exemption for holdings?<span>+</span></div><div class="dft-faq-a">Yes. If the UAE company holds ≥ 5% of a subsidiary for ≥ 12 months and the subsidiary is taxed at ≥ 9% (or equivalent substance), received dividends are exempt (Art. 22 of Federal Decree-Law No. 47 of 2022).</div></div>
      <div class="dft-faq-item"><div class="dft-faq-q">Does the UAE have a tax treaty with France?<span>+</span></div><div class="dft-faq-a">Yes, treaty of 19/07/1989. UAE-source dividends are taxable in France but benefit from a deemed foreign tax credit. For certified UAE tax residents (TRC), French exemption applies.</div></div>
    </div>
  </section>
