<script>
(function(){
  var root = document.getElementById('dftDivDist');
  if(!root) return;


  // Force English by default, ignore any saved preference
  var currentLang = 'en';


  function $(id){ return document.getElementById(id); }
  function n(id){ return parseFloat($(id).value) || 0; }
  function fmt(v){ return Math.round(v).toLocaleString(currentLang === 'en' ? 'en-US' : 'fr-FR'); }
  function escapeHtml(s){
    return String(s).replace(/[&<>"']/g, function(c){
      return {'&':'&amp;','<':'&lt;','>':'&gt;','"':'&quot;',"'":'&#39;'}[c];
    });
  }


  var countryTax = {
    ae: {individual:0, corporate:0, name_fr:'UAE', name_en:'UAE', desc_fr:'TRC requis', desc_en:'TRC required'},
    fr: {individual:0.30, corporate:0.25, name_fr:'France', name_en:'France', desc_fr:'PFU 30% particulier / IS 25% société', desc_en:'PFU 30% individual / CIT 25% company'},
    be: {individual:0.30, corporate:0.25, name_fr:'Belgique', name_en:'Belgium', desc_fr:'Précompte mobilier 30%', desc_en:'Withholding 30%'},
    lu: {individual:0.25, corporate:0.0, name_fr:'Luxembourg', name_en:'Luxembourg', desc_fr:'Régime parent-filiale société', desc_en:'Parent-subsidiary for companies'},
    ca: {individual:0.33, corporate:0.15, name_fr:'Canada', name_en:'Canada', desc_fr:'Imposition marginale + DTT', desc_en:'Marginal + DTT'},
    other: {individual:0.25, corporate:0.15, name_fr:'Autre', name_en:'Other', desc_fr:'Estimation 25% / 15%', desc_en:'Estimate 25% / 15%'}
  };


  function setLang(l){
    currentLang = l;
    root.setAttribute('data-lang', l);
    root.querySelectorAll('[data-fr]').forEach(function(el){
      var v = el.getAttribute('data-'+l);
      if(v !== null) el.innerHTML = v;
    });
    root.querySelectorAll('.dft-lang-btn').forEach(function(b){
      b.classList.toggle('active', b.getAttribute('data-lang') === l);
    });
    compute();
  }


  function compute(){
    var ebt = n('dftEbt');
    var regime = $('dftRegime').value;
    var reservePct = n('dftReserve') / 100;
    var payoutPct = n('dftPayout') / 100;
    var shType = $('dftShType').value;
    var country = $('dftCountry').value;
    var l = currentLang;


    var ct = 0;
    if(regime === 'standard') ct = Math.max(ebt - 375000, 0) * 0.09;


    var netProfit = ebt - ct;
    var reserve = netProfit * reservePct;
    var distributable = netProfit - reserve;
    var dividendGross = distributable * payoutPct;
    var wht = 0;
    var ctry = countryTax[country];
    var foreignRate = shType === 'corporate' ? ctry.corporate : ctry.individual;
    var foreignTax = dividendGross * foreignRate;
    var netPocket = dividendGross - wht - foreignTax;
    var effectiveRate = ebt > 0 ? ((ebt - netPocket) / ebt * 100) : 0;
    var retained = reserve + distributable * (1 - payoutPct);


    $('dftResMain').textContent = 'AED ' + fmt(netPocket);
    $('dftResSub').textContent = (l === 'fr' ? 'Taux effectif global : ' : 'Global effective rate: ') + effectiveRate.toFixed(1) + '%';


    var labels = l === 'fr' ? {
      ebt:'Bénéfice avant impôt', ct:'- Corporate Tax UAE',
      reg: regime === 'standard' ? 'Standard 9%' : (regime === 'sbr' ? 'SBR 0%' : 'QFZP 0%'),
      np:'Bénéfice net', res:'- Réserve légale', dist:'Résultat distribuable',
      pay:'Dividende brut distribué', wht:'- WHT UAE (0%)',
      ft:'- Impôt résidence', ft2:'Net en poche', ret:'Retenu en société'
    } : {
      ebt:'Profit before tax', ct:'- UAE Corporate Tax',
      reg: regime === 'standard' ? 'Standard 9%' : (regime === 'sbr' ? 'SBR 0%' : 'QFZP 0%'),
      np:'Net profit', res:'- Legal reserve', dist:'Distributable result',
      pay:'Gross dividend declared', wht:'- UAE WHT (0%)',
      ft:'- Residence tax', ft2:'Net in pocket', ret:'Retained in company'
    };
    var ctryName = l === 'en' ? ctry.name_en : ctry.name_fr;
    var ctryDesc = l === 'en' ? ctry.desc_en : ctry.desc_fr;


    $('dftFlowViz').innerHTML =
      '<div class="dft-flow-step active"><div class="dft-flow-label">' + labels.ebt + '</div><div class="dft-flow-value">' + fmt(ebt) + '</div></div>' +
      '<div class="dft-flow-step out"><div class="dft-flow-label">' + labels.ct + ' (' + labels.reg + ')</div><div class="dft-flow-value out">-' + fmt(ct) + '</div></div>' +
      '<div class="dft-flow-step active"><div class="dft-flow-label">' + labels.np + '</div><div class="dft-flow-value">' + fmt(netProfit) + '</div></div>' +
      '<div class="dft-flow-step out"><div class="dft-flow-label">' + labels.res + ' (' + n('dftReserve') + '%)</div><div class="dft-flow-value out">-' + fmt(reserve) + '</div></div>' +
      '<div class="dft-flow-step active"><div class="dft-flow-label">' + labels.dist + '</div><div class="dft-flow-value">' + fmt(distributable) + '</div></div>' +
      '<div class="dft-flow-step active"><div class="dft-flow-label">' + labels.pay + ' (' + n('dftPayout') + '%)</div><div class="dft-flow-value">' + fmt(dividendGross) + '</div></div>' +
      '<div class="dft-flow-step"><div class="dft-flow-label">' + labels.wht + '</div><div class="dft-flow-value">0</div></div>' +
      '<div class="dft-flow-step out"><div class="dft-flow-label">' + labels.ft + ' (' + escapeHtml(ctryName) + ' · ' + (foreignRate * 100).toFixed(0) + '%)</div><div class="dft-flow-value out">-' + fmt(foreignTax) + '</div></div>' +
      '<div class="dft-flow-step active"><div class="dft-flow-label">' + labels.ft2 + '</div><div class="dft-flow-value in">AED ' + fmt(netPocket) + '</div></div>';


    $('dftBreakdown').innerHTML =
      '<div class="dft-result-row"><span>' + (l === 'fr' ? 'Pays résidence' : 'Country of residence') + '</span><span class="dft-val">' + escapeHtml(ctryName) + '</span></div>' +
      '<div class="dft-result-row"><span>' + (l === 'fr' ? 'Taux IR applicable' : 'Applicable income tax') + '</span><span class="dft-val">' + (foreignRate * 100).toFixed(0) + '% · ' + escapeHtml(ctryDesc) + '</span></div>' +
      '<div class="dft-result-row"><span>' + labels.ret + '</span><span class="dft-val">' + fmt(retained) + '</span></div>' +
      '<div class="dft-result-row dft-highlight"><span>' + labels.ft2 + '</span><span class="dft-val">AED ' + fmt(netPocket) + '</span></div>';
  }


  // Lang buttons
  root.querySelectorAll('.dft-lang-btn').forEach(function(b){
    b.addEventListener('click', function(){ setLang(b.getAttribute('data-lang')); });
  });


  // FAQ
  root.querySelectorAll('.dft-faq-item').forEach(function(item){
    item.addEventListener('click', function(){ item.classList.toggle('open'); });
  });


  // Live compute
  ['dftEbt','dftRegime','dftReserve','dftPayout','dftShType','dftCountry'].forEach(function(id){
    var el = $(id);
    el.addEventListener('input', compute);
    el.addEventListener('change', compute);
  });


  setLang(currentLang);
})();
</script>

  <section class="dft-seo">
    <div class="dft-lang-fr">
      <h2>Facturation conforme aux <span>Émirats Arabes Unis</span></h2>
      <p>Aux UAE, toute société enregistrée à la VAT doit émettre une Tax Invoice conforme à l'article 59 du règlement exécutif du Federal Decree-Law No. 8 of 2017. Les mentions obligatoires : "Tax Invoice", TRN émetteur et client, date d'émission, numéro séquentiel, description, montant HT, VAT 5%, total TTC.</p>
      <h3>Mentions obligatoires</h3>
      <ul><li>Mention claire "Tax Invoice"</li><li>Nom, adresse et TRN du fournisseur</li><li>Nom, adresse du client, TRN si enregistré VAT</li><li>Numéro séquentiel unique</li><li>Date d'émission et date de fourniture</li><li>Description, quantité, prix unitaire</li><li>Montant HT, taux et montant VAT, total TTC</li></ul>
      <h3>FAQ</h3>
      <div class="dft-faq-item"><div class="dft-faq-q">Tax Invoice vs Simplified Tax Invoice ?<span>+</span></div><div class="dft-faq-a">La Simplified est autorisée pour B2C &lt; AED 10 000. Moins de mentions (pas de TRN client). Au-delà ou en B2B, la Tax Invoice complète est obligatoire.</div></div>
      <div class="dft-faq-item"><div class="dft-faq-q">Durée de conservation des factures ?<span>+</span></div><div class="dft-faq-a">5 ans minimum (15 ans pour l'immobilier). Format électronique accepté.</div></div>
      <div class="dft-faq-item"><div class="dft-faq-q">Tous les biens et services sont-ils à 5% ?<span>+</span></div><div class="dft-faq-a">Non. Zero-rated : exports hors GCC, médicaments, transport international. Exemptés : services financiers, location résidentielle long terme.</div></div>
      <div class="dft-faq-item"><div class="dft-faq-q">Facturation en USD ou EUR possible ?<span>+</span></div><div class="dft-faq-a">Oui, mais la VAT doit être exprimée en AED au taux officiel UAE Central Bank à la date d'émission.</div></div>
    </div>
    <div class="dft-lang-en">
      <h2>UAE <span>Tax Invoice</span> compliance</h2>
      <p>In the UAE, every VAT-registered company must issue a Tax Invoice compliant with Article 59 of the Executive Regulation of Federal Decree-Law No. 8 of 2017. Mandatory mentions: "Tax Invoice", issuer and customer TRN, issue date, sequential number, description, net amount, VAT 5%, total.</p>
      <h3>Mandatory information</h3>
      <ul><li>Clear "Tax Invoice" header</li><li>Supplier name, address and TRN</li><li>Customer name, address, TRN if VAT-registered</li><li>Unique sequential invoice number</li><li>Issue date and supply date</li><li>Description, quantity, unit price</li><li>Net amount, VAT rate and amount, total</li></ul>
      <h3>FAQ</h3>
      <div class="dft-faq-item"><div class="dft-faq-q">Tax Invoice vs Simplified Tax Invoice?<span>+</span></div><div class="dft-faq-a">The Simplified is allowed for B2C below AED 10,000. Fewer fields (no customer TRN). Above that threshold or for B2B, the full Tax Invoice is mandatory.</div></div>
      <div class="dft-faq-item"><div class="dft-faq-q">Invoice retention period?<span>+</span></div><div class="dft-faq-a">Minimum 5 years (15 years for real estate). Electronic format accepted.</div></div>
      <div class="dft-faq-item"><div class="dft-faq-q">Are all goods and services taxed at 5%?<span>+</span></div><div class="dft-faq-a">No. Zero-rated: exports outside GCC, medicines, international transport. Exempt: financial services, long-term residential rentals.</div></div>
      <div class="dft-faq-item"><div class="dft-faq-q">Can I invoice in USD or EUR?<span>+</span></div><div class="dft-faq-a">Yes, but VAT must be shown in AED using the official UAE Central Bank rate on issue date.</div></div>
    </div>
  </section>


  <div class="dft-cta">

    <p data-fr="Daftime gère votre enregistrement FTA, vos déclarations trimestrielles et vos audits VAT." data-en="Daftime manages your FTA registration, quarterly VAT returns and audits.">Daftime gère votre enregistrement FTA, vos déclarations trimestrielles et vos audits VAT.</p>

<script>
(function(){
  var root = document.getElementById('dftInvGen');
  if(!root) return;


  var currentLang = 'fr';
  try {
    var saved = localStorage.getItem('daftime_lang');
    if(saved) currentLang = saved;
    else if(navigator.language && navigator.language.indexOf('en')===0) currentLang = 'en';
  } catch(e){}


  var items = [{desc:'',qty:1,price:0}];


  function $(id){ return document.getElementById(id); }


  function setLang(l){
    currentLang = l;
    root.setAttribute('data-lang', l);
    try { localStorage.setItem('daftime_lang', l); } catch(e){}
    root.querySelectorAll('[data-fr]').forEach(function(el){
      var v = el.getAttribute('data-'+l);
      if(v !== null) el.innerHTML = v;
    });
    root.querySelectorAll('.dft-lang-btn').forEach(function(b){
      b.classList.toggle('active', b.getAttribute('data-lang') === l);
    });
    renderItems();
    render();
  }


  function renderItems(){
    var phDesc = currentLang === 'fr' ? 'Description' : 'Description';
    var phQty = currentLang === 'fr' ? 'Qté' : 'Qty';
    var phPrice = currentLang === 'fr' ? 'Prix U.' : 'Unit price';
    var html = items.map(function(it, i){
      var total = (it.qty * it.price).toFixed(2);
      return '<div class="dft-item-row">' +
        '<input type="text" class="dft-form-input" placeholder="' + phDesc + '" value="' + escapeHtml(it.desc) + '" data-idx="' + i + '" data-field="desc">' +
        '<input type="number" class="dft-form-input" placeholder="' + phQty + '" value="' + it.qty + '" data-idx="' + i + '" data-field="qty">' +
        '<input type="number" class="dft-form-input" placeholder="' + phPrice + '" value="' + it.price + '" data-idx="' + i + '" data-field="price">' +
        '<input type="text" class="dft-form-input" value="' + total + '" readonly>' +
        '<button type="button" class="dft-btn-remove" data-remove="' + i + '">×</button>' +
      '</div>';
    }).join('');
    $('dftItems').innerHTML = html;
    $('dftItems').querySelectorAll('input[data-idx]').forEach(function(inp){
      inp.addEventListener('input', function(){
        var idx = parseInt(inp.getAttribute('data-idx'), 10);
        var field = inp.getAttribute('data-field');
        items[idx][field] = field === 'desc' ? inp.value : (parseFloat(inp.value) || 0);
        render();
        if(field !== 'desc') {
          var row = inp.parentElement;
          var totalInput = row.querySelectorAll('input')[3];
          totalInput.value = (items[idx].qty * items[idx].price).toFixed(2);
        }
      });
    });
    $('dftItems').querySelectorAll('[data-remove]').forEach(function(btn){
      btn.addEventListener('click', function(){
        var idx = parseInt(btn.getAttribute('data-remove'), 10);
        items.splice(idx, 1);
        if(items.length === 0) items.push({desc:'',qty:1,price:0});
        renderItems();
        render();
      });
    });
  }


  function escapeHtml(s){
    return String(s).replace(/[&<>"']/g, function(c){
      return {'&':'&amp;','<':'&lt;','>':'&gt;','"':'&quot;',"'":'&#39;'}[c];
    });
  }


  function render(){
    var cn = $('dftCompanyName').value;
    if(cn && $('dftPreviewLogo').style.display === 'none'){
      $('dftPreviewBrand').textContent = cn;
      $('dftPreviewBrand').style.display = 'block';
    } else if(!cn){
      $('dftPreviewBrand').style.display = 'none';
    }
    var trn = $('dftCompanyTrn').value;
    var addr = $('dftCompanyAddress').value;
    var email = $('dftCompanyEmail').value;
    var phone = $('dftCompanyPhone').value;
    $('dftPreviewFrom').innerHTML = '<strong>' + escapeHtml(cn||'') + '</strong><br>' + escapeHtml(addr||'') + '<br>' + (trn ? 'TRN: ' + escapeHtml(trn) : '') + '<br>' + escapeHtml(email||'') + ' ' + (phone ? ' · ' + escapeHtml(phone) : '');
    var clName = $('dftClientName').value;
    var clTrn = $('dftClientTrn').value;
    var clAddr = $('dftClientAddress').value;
    $('dftPreviewTo').innerHTML = '<strong>' + escapeHtml(clName||'') + '</strong><br>' + escapeHtml(clAddr||'') + '<br>' + (clTrn ? 'TRN: ' + escapeHtml(clTrn) : '');
    $('dftPreviewNum').textContent = $('dftInvoiceNum').value;
    var fmt = function(d){ return d ? new Date(d).toLocaleDateString(currentLang === 'en' ? 'en-GB' : 'fr-FR') : ''; };
    $('dftPreviewDate').textContent = fmt($('dftInvoiceDate').value);
    $('dftPreviewDue').textContent = fmt($('dftDueDate').value);
    var cur = $('dftCurrency').value;
    var sub = 0;
    $('dftPreviewItems').innerHTML = items.map(function(it){
      var t = it.qty * it.price; sub += t;
      return '<tr><td>' + escapeHtml(it.desc||'') + '</td><td>' + it.qty + '</td><td>' + it.price.toFixed(2) + ' ' + cur + '</td><td>' + t.toFixed(2) + ' ' + cur + '</td></tr>';
    }).join('');
    var vat = sub * 0.05;
    $('dftPreviewSub').textContent = sub.toFixed(2) + ' ' + cur;
    $('dftPreviewVat').textContent = vat.toFixed(2) + ' ' + cur;
    $('dftPreviewTotal').textContent = (sub + vat).toFixed(2) + ' ' + cur;
  }


  // Init dates
  $('dftInvoiceDate').valueAsDate = new Date();
  var due = new Date(); due.setDate(due.getDate() + 30);
  $('dftDueDate').valueAsDate = due;


  // Logo upload
  $('dftLogoInput').addEventListener('change', function(e){
    var f = e.target.files[0]; if(!f) return;
    var r = new FileReader();
    r.onload = function(ev){
      $('dftLogoPreview').src = ev.target.result;
      $('dftLogoPreview').style.display = 'block';
      $('dftLogoText').style.display = 'none';
      $('dftPreviewLogo').src = ev.target.result;
      $('dftPreviewLogo').style.display = 'block';
      $('dftPreviewBrand').style.display = 'none';
    };
    r.readAsDataURL(f);
  });


  // Add item
  $('dftBtnAdd').addEventListener('click', function(){
    items.push({desc:'',qty:1,price:0});
    renderItems();
    render();
  });


  // Lang buttons
  root.querySelectorAll('.dft-lang-btn').forEach(function(b){
    b.addEventListener('click', function(){ setLang(b.getAttribute('data-lang')); });
  });


  // FAQ
  root.querySelectorAll('.dft-faq-item').forEach(function(item){
    item.addEventListener('click', function(){ item.classList.toggle('open'); });
  });


  // Live render on input
  ['dftCompanyName','dftCompanyTrn','dftCompanyAddress','dftCompanyEmail','dftCompanyPhone','dftClientName','dftClientTrn','dftClientAddress','dftInvoiceNum','dftInvoiceDate','dftDueDate','dftCurrency'].forEach(function(id){
    var el = $(id);
    el.addEventListener('input', render);
    el.addEventListener('change', render);
  });


  // PDF export
  $('dftBtnExport').addEventListener('click', async function(){
    if(typeof window.jspdf === 'undefined' || typeof window.html2canvas === 'undefined'){
      alert(currentLang === 'fr' ? 'Librairie PDF non chargée. Réessayez dans un instant.' : 'PDF library not loaded. Try again in a moment.');
      return;
    }
    try {
      var jsPDF = window.jspdf.jsPDF;
      var canvas = await window.html2canvas($('dftPreview'), {scale:2, backgroundColor:'#ffffff'});
      var pdf = new jsPDF({unit:'mm', format:'a4'});
      var w = pdf.internal.pageSize.getWidth();
      var h = (canvas.height * w) / canvas.width;
      pdf.addImage(canvas.toDataURL('image/png'), 'PNG', 0, 0, w, h);
      pdf.save($('dftInvoiceNum').value + '.pdf');
    } catch(err){
      console.error(err);
      alert(currentLang === 'fr' ? 'Erreur lors de la génération du PDF.' : 'Error generating PDF.');
    }
  });


  // Init
  setLang(currentLang);
})();
</script>

  <section class="dft-seo">
    <div class="dft-lang-fr">
      <h2>La <span>TVA (VAT)</span> aux Émirats Arabes Unis</h2>
      <p>La VAT (Value Added Tax) a été introduite aux UAE le 1er janvier 2018 au taux standard de 5%, l'un des plus bas au monde. Elle est administrée par la Federal Tax Authority (FTA) selon le Federal Decree-Law No. 8 of 2017.</p>
      <h3>Les 3 taux possibles</h3>
      <ul><li><strong>5% standard</strong> : biens et services généraux</li><li><strong>0% zero-rated</strong> : exports hors GCC, transport international, médicaments, premier transfert immobilier résidentiel neuf, éducation et santé sous conditions</li><li><strong>Exempt</strong> : services financiers non rémunérés explicitement, location résidentielle long terme, transport local de passagers</li></ul>
      <h3>Le Reverse Charge Mechanism (RCM)</h3>
      <p>Le Reverse Charge s'applique notamment aux importations de services depuis l'étranger : le client UAE doit s'auto-liquider la VAT (sortie) et la déduire (entrée) sur la même déclaration. Neutre en trésorerie si pro-rata 100%.</p>
      <h3>FAQ</h3>
      <div class="dft-faq-item"><div class="dft-faq-q">À partir de quel chiffre d'affaires s'enregistrer ?<span>+</span></div><div class="dft-faq-a">Obligation dès AED 375 000 de chiffre d'affaires taxable sur 12 mois. Enregistrement volontaire possible dès AED 187 500.</div></div>
      <div class="dft-faq-item"><div class="dft-faq-q">Fréquence des déclarations VAT ?<span>+</span></div><div class="dft-faq-a">Trimestrielle par défaut (Form 201), mensuelle pour les CA &gt; AED 150M. Deadline : 28 jours après la fin de la période.</div></div>
    </div>
    <div class="dft-lang-en">
      <h2><span>VAT</span> in the United Arab Emirates</h2>
      <p>VAT was introduced in the UAE on 1 January 2018 at a standard rate of 5%, one of the lowest worldwide. It is administered by the Federal Tax Authority (FTA) under Federal Decree-Law No. 8 of 2017.</p>
      <h3>The 3 possible rates</h3>
      <ul><li><strong>5% standard</strong>: most goods and services</li><li><strong>0% zero-rated</strong>: exports outside the GCC, international transport, medicines, first supply of new residential real estate, education and healthcare under conditions</li><li><strong>Exempt</strong>: unremunerated financial services, long-term residential rentals, local passenger transport</li></ul>
      <h3>Reverse Charge Mechanism (RCM)</h3>
      <p>Reverse Charge notably applies to services imported from abroad: the UAE client self-assesses output VAT and reclaims input VAT on the same return. Cash-neutral if pro-rata is 100%.</p>
      <h3>FAQ</h3>
      <div class="dft-faq-item"><div class="dft-faq-q">At what turnover must I register?<span>+</span></div><div class="dft-faq-a">Mandatory above AED 375,000 taxable turnover over 12 months. Voluntary registration from AED 187,500.</div></div>
      <div class="dft-faq-item"><div class="dft-faq-q">How often must I file?<span>+</span></div><div class="dft-faq-a">Quarterly by default (Form 201), monthly above AED 150M turnover. Deadline: 28 days after period end.</div></div>
    </div>
  </section>

<script>
(function(){
  var root = document.getElementById('dftVatCalc');
  if(!root) return;


  var currentLang = 'fr';
  var mode = 'ht';


  try {
    var saved = localStorage.getItem('daftime_lang');
    if(saved) currentLang = saved;
    else if(navigator.language && navigator.language.indexOf('en')===0) currentLang = 'en';
  } catch(e){}


  function $(id){ return document.getElementById(id); }
  function fmt(v){ return Math.round(v).toLocaleString(currentLang === 'en' ? 'en-US' : 'fr-FR'); }


  function setLang(l){
    currentLang = l;
    root.setAttribute('data-lang', l);
    try { localStorage.setItem('daftime_lang', l); } catch(e){}
    root.querySelectorAll('[data-fr]').forEach(function(el){
      var v = el.getAttribute('data-'+l);
      if(v !== null) el.innerHTML = v;
    });
    root.querySelectorAll('.dft-lang-btn').forEach(function(b){
      b.classList.toggle('active', b.getAttribute('data-lang') === l);
    });
    compute();
  }


  function compute(){
    var amt = parseFloat($('dftAmount').value) || 0;
    var rate = parseFloat($('dftRate').value) || 0;
    var l = currentLang;
    var ht = 0, vat = 0, ttc = 0, label = '', sub = '';


    if(mode === 'ht'){
      ht = amt; vat = amt * rate / 100; ttc = amt + vat;
      $('dftLblAmount').textContent = l === 'fr' ? 'Montant HT (AED)' : 'Net amount (AED)';
      label = l === 'fr' ? 'Montant TTC' : 'Gross amount';
      sub = (l === 'fr' ? 'VAT incluse : ' : 'VAT included: ') + fmt(vat) + ' AED';
    } else if(mode === 'ttc'){
      ttc = amt; ht = amt / (1 + rate / 100); vat = amt - ht;
      $('dftLblAmount').textContent = l === 'fr' ? 'Montant TTC (AED)' : 'Gross amount (AED)';
      label = l === 'fr' ? 'Montant HT' : 'Net amount';
      sub = (l === 'fr' ? 'VAT à déduire : ' : 'Extractable VAT: ') + fmt(vat) + ' AED';
    } else {
      ht = amt; vat = amt * rate / 100; ttc = ht;
      $('dftLblAmount').textContent = l === 'fr' ? 'Valeur service importé (AED)' : 'Imported service value (AED)';
      label = l === 'fr' ? 'Reverse Charge neutre' : 'Reverse Charge neutral';
      sub = (l === 'fr' ? 'Output VAT auto-liquidée : ' : 'Self-assessed output VAT: ') + fmt(vat) + ' AED';
    }


    $('dftResLabel').textContent = label;
    $('dftResMain').textContent = 'AED ' + fmt(mode === 'ttc' ? ht : ttc);
    $('dftResSub').textContent = sub;
    $('dftRHt').textContent = fmt(ht);
    $('dftRVat').textContent = fmt(vat);
    $('dftRTtc').textContent = fmt(ttc);
  }


  // Tab buttons
  root.querySelectorAll('.dft-tab').forEach(function(t){
    t.addEventListener('click', function(){
      root.querySelectorAll('.dft-tab').forEach(function(x){ x.classList.remove('active'); });
      t.classList.add('active');
      mode = t.getAttribute('data-mode');
      compute();
    });
  });


  // Lang buttons
  root.querySelectorAll('.dft-lang-btn').forEach(function(b){
    b.addEventListener('click', function(){ setLang(b.getAttribute('data-lang')); });
  });


  // FAQ
  root.querySelectorAll('.dft-faq-item').forEach(function(item){
    item.addEventListener('click', function(){ item.classList.toggle('open'); });
  });


  // Live compute
  $('dftAmount').addEventListener('input', compute);
  $('dftRate').addEventListener('change', compute);


  setLang(currentLang);
})();
</script>
